Question #1 (ID: 209503)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The graph below, shows the selling rates of seven types of books in 'Ekushey Boi Mela-2023'. Describe the graph highlighting the information given in the bar chart:


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans. The graph illustrates the selling rates of seven types of books in Ekushey Boi Mela-2023. In the graph, we can see that only 500 copies of research related books were sold. On the other hand, thousand copies of poetry books were bought by the customers. Interestingly, a sharp rise is seen in the number of sold novel books. The sold copies of novel reads 4700 which is the highest in the graph. Moreover, 2000 copies of history related books, 1500 copies of travel related books and 2500 copies of comics were sold in the fair. Book based on drama lies at the bottom with the lowest selling number. Only 400 copies of drama books were bought by the customers. From the graph, we see that novel books are popular among the readers as it is the highest selling book-type.

Explanation:
বেরি: চার্টটি 'একুশে বই মেলা‑2023'-এ সাত ধরনের বইয়ের বিক্রয় হার দেখায়; প্রতিটি বার তার বিভাগের বিক্রয় পরিমাণকে উপস্থাপন করছে। সঠিক উত্তরটি বারগুলোর উচ্চতা ও অনুভূমিক/উভয় অক্ষের সংখ্যাগত মান দেখে নিরূপণ করা যায় — সর্বোচ্চ উচ্চতার বারটি সবচেয়ে বেশি বিক্রি এবং সর্বনিম্ন উচ্চতার বারটি সবচেয়ে কম বিক্রি নির্দেশ করে, আর মাঝের বারগুলোর তুলনা করে অংশগুলোর অনুপাত বোঝা যায়।

Question #2 (ID: 209504)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
I will arise and go now, and go to Innisfree,

And a small cabin build there, of clay and wattles made;

Nine bean rows will I have there, a hive for the honey bee

And live alone in the bee loud glade.

And I shall have some peace there, for peace comes dropping slow

Dropping from the veils of the moing to where the cricket sings;

There midnight’s all a glimmer, and noon a purple glow,

And evening full of the linnet’s wings.

I will arise and go now, for always night and day

I hear lake water lapping with low sounds by the shore;

While I stand on the roadway, or on the pavements grey,

I hear it in the deep heart’s core.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Escaping to Innisfree's tranquil beauty. A rustic cabin amidst nature's embrace, cultivating life with bees and beans. Peace trickles from morning veils, where crickets and birds compose serene melodies. The allure persists day and night, the lake's gentle lap echoing in the heart's core.

Explanation:
Explanation: The correct answer—that the poem expresses a longing for peace and escape to nature—is supported by the speaker’s repeated resolution “I will arise and go” and the simple rural images (cabin, bean rows, hive) that contrast with “pavements grey.” Yeats’s use of sensory details (lake water lapping, midnight’s glimmer) and repetition shows an inward yearning: the external peaceful landscape mirrors and soothes the speaker’s “deep heart’s core,” which explains the poem’s pastoral, escapist theme.

Question #3 (ID: 209505)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
I died for beauty, but was scarce
Adjusted in the tomb,
When one who died for truth was lain
In an adjoining room.

He questioned softly why I failed?
“For beauty,” I replied.
“And I for truth, -the two are one;
We brethren are,” he said.

And so, as kinsmen met a night,
We talked between the rooms,
Until the moss had reached our lips,
And covered up our names.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Harmonious convergence of Beauty and Truth in Death. The poem narrates a posthumous encounter between souls—one who died for beauty and the other for truth. Their dialogue reveals a shared essence, highlighting the interconnectedness of these concepts. The gradual covering of their names with moss signifies the dissolution of individual identities, emphasizing the unity of values beyond life's divisions.

Explanation:
The poem shows that the speaker (who “died for beauty”) and the neighbor (who “died for truth”) are essentially the same kind of martyr, so the correct answer—that beauty and truth are kindred or unified—is right. Dickinson uses simple dialogue, personification, and burial imagery (the adjoining rooms, the moss covering their lips and names) to show that death equalizes them and reveals their close relationship. The underlying idea is that abstract ideals like beauty and truth can demand sacrifice and, in the end, are joined rather than opposed.

Question #4 (ID: 209506)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
I sit on one of the dives

On Fifty-second Street

Uncertain and afraid

As the clever hopes expire.

Of a low dishonest decade:

Waves of anger and fear

Circulate over the bright

And darkened lands of the earth,

Obsessing our private lives;

The unmentionable odour of death

Offends the September night.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Turbulent reflections on an era's moral decay. Amidst uncertainty and fear, the speaker contemplates a deceitful decade marked by anger, fear, and fading optimism. Global turmoil intrudes on personal spheres, and the sinister shadow of mortality taints the very air, symbolizing the discomforting truth of a troubled world.

Explanation:
The correct answer — that the poem expresses post‑war disillusionment, fear, and moral decay — is right because words and phrases like "a low dishonest decade," "waves of anger and fear," and "the unmentionable odour of death" directly name corruption, pervasive anxiety, and the presence of death. Eliot’s terse, fragmented images (the city street, “obsessing our private lives,” the September night) create a mood of isolation and despair that reflects the broader historical context and the poem’s theme of spiritual and social breakdown.

Question #5 (ID: 209507)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
I will arise and go now, and go to Innisfree,

And a small cabin build there, of clay and wattles made;

Nine bean rows will I have there, a hive for the honey bee

And live alone in the bee loud glade.

And I shall have some peace there, for peace comes dropping slow

Dropping from the veils of the morning to where the cricket sings;

There midnight’s all a glimmer, and noon a purple glow,

And evening full of the linnet’s wings.

I will arise and go now, for always night and day

I hear lake water lapping with low sounds by the shore;

While I stand on the roadway, or on the pavements grey,

I hear it in the deep heart’s core.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Longing for a simpler, tranquil existence. The narrator expresses a desire to escape the chaos of urban life and retreat to a peaceful haven in Innisfree. The depiction of nature's serene beauty and harmonious sounds contrasts with the urban clamor, highlighting the yearning for inner peace and connection with the natural world.

Explanation:
The correct answer is that the poem expresses the speaker’s deep longing to leave the city and live in simple, peaceful communion with nature. Lines about building a cabin, planting bean rows and hearing “lake water lapping” use sensory imagery to show the restful, restorative life he imagines, while the contrast with “pavements grey” and the repeated “I will arise and go now” emphasize both his dissatisfaction with urban life and his firm desire to escape to that peace.

Question #6 (ID: 209508)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
I wandered lonely as a cloud

That floats on high o’er vales and hills,

When all at once I saw a crowd,

A host, of golden daffodils;

Beside the lake, beneath the trees,

Fluttering and dancing in the breeze,

Continuous as the stars that shine

And twinkle on the Milky Way,

They stretched in never-ending line

Along the margin of a bay:

Ten thousand saw I at a glance,

Tossing their heads in sprightly dance.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Nature's transformative power on emotions. The speaker's initial isolation gives way to enchantment upon encountering a field of daffodils. The flowers' vibrant beauty and rhythmic movement evoke a sense of awe, symbolising the capacity of nature to uplift the spirit and alleviate loneliness through moments of profound connection and beauty.

Explanation:
The opening line is a simile—“as a cloud” directly compares the poet’s solitary wandering to a cloud, showing lightness and detachment. The daffodils are personified (“fluttering and dancing,” “tossing their heads”), which gives them lively, human action and creates a joyful mood. The phrase “Ten thousand” is hyperbolic to emphasize the vast number and the overwhelming, uplifting effect the sight has on the speaker.

Question #7 (ID: 209509)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
My heart leaps up when I behold

Or let me die!

The child is father of the Man:

A rainbow in the sky:

And I could wish my days to be

So was it when my life began;

Bound each to each by natural piety.

So is it now I am a man;

So be it when I shall grow old,

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Eternal connection of youth and age. Awe at nature's beauty sustains through life's stages. Childhood's wonder shapes adulthood's perspective, and the promise of a vivid future endures even in old age, bound by innate reverence for life's unity.

Explanation:
The correct answer is right because the poem’s lines consistently show one idea: the speaker’s spontaneous joy at seeing a rainbow continues unchanged from childhood into adulthood and old age. The phrase "The child is father of the Man" and the repeating lines "So was it when my life began; / So is it now I am a man; / So be it when I shall grow old" support the concept that early feelings shape later life and that a natural, reverent attachment to nature persists across life stages. This explains why the theme of continuity of childlike wonder and "natural piety" is the central idea.

Question #8 (ID: 209510)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
If you fail to see the person

But only see the disability.

Then who is blind?

If you cannot hear

Your brother’s Cry for justice,

Who is deaf?

If you do not communicate

With your sister

But separate her from you

Who is the mentally handicapped?

If you do not stand up

For the rights of all persons

Who is crippled

Your attitude

Towards persons with disabilities

May be our biggest handicap

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Challenging perceptions of disability. The narrative highlights the real limitations lie in misconceptions and biases. The story underscores that those who fail to see the person beyond their disability are the ones truly impaired. Lack of empathy, communication, and advocacy results in society's biggest handicap - an attitude that hinders inclusivity and equal rights for persons with disabilities.

Explanation:
Explanation: The poem shows that ignoring a person’s humanity, refusing to listen or include them, and not standing up for their rights are the real barriers — so “your attitude” is the biggest handicap. This reflects the social model of disability: people are disabled more by society’s prejudice and exclusion than by their physical or mental differences.

Question #9 (ID: 209511)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Hold fast to dreams

For if dreams die

Life is a broken-winged bird

That cannot fly.

Hold fast to dreams

For when dreams go

Life is a barren field

Frozen with snow.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The fragility and significance of dreams. The verses underscore the importance of holding onto one's aspirations, as they provide the motivation and vitality that enable a fulfilling life. The comparison of life without dreams to a bird with broken wings or a barren frozen field conveys the desolation and lack of purpose that comes from abandoning one's dreams.

Explanation:
The poem’s central message is to hold on to dreams because without them life loses purpose and vitality. The images of a “broken‑winged bird” and a “barren field frozen with snow” are metaphors showing that when dreams die, a person becomes unable to soar and their life becomes sterile and lifeless.

Question #10 (ID: 209512)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Sylhet Board, Dhaka Board, Dinajpur Board | Tags: Sylhet Board, Jessore Board, Dhaka Board, Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Time, you old gipsy man,

Will you not stay?

Put up your caravan Just for one day?

All things I’ll give you,

Will you be my guest?

Bells for your jennet or silver the best.

Goldsmiths will beat you

A great golden ring.

Peacocks will bow to you,

Little boys sing,

Oh, and sweet girls will

Festoon you with may.

Time, you old gipsy. Why hasten away?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ephemeral nature of time and longing for its pause. The speaker appeals to time as a traveler, requesting a moment's respite from its ceaseless march. Material offerings symbolize the willingness to give up treasures for a fleeting moment. The verses reflect the universal desire to capture time's elusive essence and to savor life's fleeting joys before they vanish.

Explanation:
Explanation: The correct answer — that the speaker is pleading with Time to stay — is supported by direct address and imperatives like "Will you not stay? Put up your caravan Just for one day?" which show a request to halt Time. The speaker lists lavish gifts and flattering images to persuade Time, so the poem personifies Time as a "gipsy man" and treats it as someone who can be persuaded. The underlying concept is personification and the theme of trying to stop or prolong a cherished moment by offering everything one has.

Question #11 (ID: 209513)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Chittagong Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board | Tags: Cumilla Board, Chattogram Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Blow, blow, thou winter wind,

Thou art not so unkind

As man’s ingratitude;

Thy tooth is not so keen,

Because thou art not seen,

Although thy breath be rude,

Heigh-ho! sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly:

Most friendship is feigning, most loving mere folly:

Then heigh-ho, the holly!

This life is most jolly.

Freeze, freeze, thou bitter sky,

That dost not bite so nigh

As benefits forgot:

Though thou the waters warp,

Thy sting is not so sharp

As friend remembered not.

Heigh-hol sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly…

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The fickleness of human relationships and gratitude. Nature's harshness is compared to people's ingratitude, with winter wind and frozen sky representing forgotten kindness. The refrain "Heigh-ho" contrasts the facade of friendship and love with the underlying truth, while celebrating life's transient and unpredictable nature, emphasizing the bittersweet reality of existence.

Explanation:
The correct reading is that the poet finds human ingratitude and false friendship worse than the harshness of winter. Lines like "Thy tooth is not so keen" and "benefits forgot... friend remembered not" show he compares visible natural cold to the sharper, unseen pain of being betrayed or unthankful. The poem’s underlying idea is that human cruelty stings more than nature, so the speaker accepts the holly’s cheerfulness as a symbol of hardy constancy.

Question #12 (ID: 209514)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
O father and mother if buds are nipped,

And blossoms blown away;

And if the tender plants are stripped

Of their joy in the springing day,

By sorrow and care’s dismay,How shall the summer arise in joy?

Or the summer fruits appear?

Or how shall we gather what griefs destroy,

Or bless the mellowing year,

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The impact of adversity on growth and happiness. The story conveys the metaphor of nipped buds and stripped plants to depict how sorrow and care can hinder the blossoming of potential. The questions raised highlight the challenge of finding joy and reaping the rewards of life when early setbacks and hardships have disrupted the process.

Explanation:
Explanation: The correct answer is right because the poet uses the image of "buds nipped" and "blossoms blown away" to show how early sorrow destroys the possibility of later happiness. Buds and blossoms symbolize youthful hopes and promising beginnings, while "summer" and "summer fruits" represent maturity and reward; the rhetorical questions emphasize that if beginnings are ruined, the later joys cannot come. This links the natural imagery directly to the poem’s theme that premature loss or grief prevents future fulfillment.

Question #13 (ID: 209515)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Under the greenwood tree

Who loves to lie with me,

And turn his merry note

Unto the sweet bird’s throat

Come hither, come hither, come hither!

Here shall he see

No enemy

But winter and rough weather.

Who doth ambition shun

And loves to live i’ the sun

Seeking the food he eats

And pleased with what he gets

Come hither, come hither, come hither!

Here shall he see

No enemy

But winter and rough weather

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Embracing a simple and carefree life in nature. The story invites those who value companionship and contentment to join under the greenwood tree. Rejecting ambition, the verses celebrate finding joy in life's basic pleasures and necessities. The refrain "Come hither" emphasizes the appeal of such a life, where the only adversaries are the challenges of winter and inclement weather.

Explanation:
The correct answer is right because the speaker directly invites those who “doth ambition shun” and “loves to live i’ the sun” to come sit under the greenwood tree, promising they will find no enemies except “winter and rough weather.” This expresses the poem’s pastoral idea: it praises a simple, nature‑centered life free from worldly ambition, where only natural hardships disturb the peace.

Question:
Blow, blow, thou winter wind,

Thou art not so unkind

As man’s ingratitude:

Thy tooth is not so keen,

Because thou art not seen,

Although thy breath be rude.

Heigh-ho! sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly:

Most friendship is feigning, most loving mere folly:

Then heigh-ho, the holly!

This life is most jolly.

Freeze, freeze, thou bitter sky.

That dost not bite so nigh

As benefits forgot:

Though thou the waters warp.

Thy sting is not so sharp

As friend remembered not.

High-ho! sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly ……..

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The fickleness of human relationships and ingratitude. The verses compare the coldness of winter winds and skies to the callousness of human behavior. The refrain "Heigh-ho" laments the superficiality of friendship and love, highlighting the tendency to feign emotions. The contrast between the bitter sky and forgotten benefits emphasizes the pain of unappreciated kindness, urging remembrance and genuine connections.

Explanation:
The correct answer is that the poem says human ingratitude and false friendship are worse than the harsh winter wind. Shakespeare contrasts the cold, visible pain of winter with the deeper, more lasting hurt caused by friends who forget favors or show false affection, using the holly refrain to suggest bitter laughter and endurance. This comparison shows the poem’s central idea: emotional betrayal wounds more than physical hardship.

Question #16 (ID: 209483)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following pie chart shows the export sectors in Bangladesh that earn foreign currency. Write a paragraph describing the chart .


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans. The chart provides information of some export sectors in Bangladesh that earn foreign currency. In the chart, we can see that by exporting garments Bangladesh earns 54% of its total foreign currency. The second highest foreign currency comes froin exporting our manpower. From this sector, Bangladesh earns 30% of its total foreign currency. The contribution of tea & fish and other sources is same. From each of these sectors, Bangladesh earns 8% of its total foreign currency. So, after analyzing the chart, it can be said that garments and manpower are two important sectors that help Bangladesh earn over 80% of its foreign currency. The country should sustain this percentage by giving maximum support to these sectors.

Explanation:
বর্ণনা: চার্টে রেডি-মেড গার্মেন্টস স্পষ্টভাবে সবচেয়ে বড় কেটে দেখা যাচ্ছে, অর্থাৎ বিদেশি মুদ্রা আয়ের সবচেয়ে বড় উৎস; জুটিভিত্তিক পণ্য, চামড়া-পণ্যের মতো খাতগুলো তুলনামূলকভাবে ছোট অংশ দখল করেছে। ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক উত্তরের কারণ হলো পাইচা-এর প্রতিটি স্লাইস তার অনুপাত বা শতাংশ দেখায়, তাই সবচেয়ে বড় স্লাইসেই সবচেয়ে বেশি রাজস্ব নির্দেশ করে। অর্থনৈতিক শিক্ষা: এই চার্ট বোঝায় দেশের রপ্তানিতে এক বা দুই খাতে নির্ভরশীলতা বেশি—বৈচিত্র্য বাড়ালে রপ্তানি ও আয় আরও স্থিতিশীল হবে।

Question #17 (ID: 209482)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2023, 2017 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Cumilla Board, Dinajpur Board, Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The pie chart below shows the time allocation of a student's daily activities. Describe the chart in 150 words. You should highlight and summarize the information in the chart.


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans. The given pie chart shows the time allocation of a student's daily activities. According to the chart, the student spends most of his time in sleeping, in college and in study. He spends 75% of his total time in these three activities where sleep covers 30%, college hours 25%, and study 20%. The time allocation for recreation is 12% of his total time.

However, the student has a little time for playing, which is only 5%. Apart from these, the student has to do some other activities in which he spends 8% of his time. So, the chart shows that the student follows a daily routine.

Explanation:
The pie chart divides the student's 24‑hour day among activities, showing the largest sector for sleep, substantial portions for study and school, and smaller slices for meals, commuting and leisure. This description is correct because a pie chart represents parts of a whole—each sector’s angle and area are proportional to the time spent, so bigger sectors mean more hours. Read the sector sizes or labels to compare priorities and see how the student’s time could be redistributed if they want more study or free time.

Question #18 (ID: 209481)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The graph shows the engagement of child labour in different sectors of 'X' country from 2005 to 2016. Describe the graph in 150 words. You should highlight the main features and summarize the information given in the graph.


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans. The graph presents the engagement of the child labour in different sectors of 'X' country from 2005 to 2016. In the graph, the data shown are of three different sectors namely Agriculture, Industry and Service. The most striking feature of the graph is that with the passage of time child labour has been shifted from agriculture to Industry and Service. Actually, industrial sector has experienced a steady rise from 15 percent in 2005 to 2 percent in 2016 while service sector has seen a fluctuation having 23 percent in 2005 and 36 percent in 2012. with a fall of 5 percent in 2016. Another important point is that agriculture has had a great fall from 62 percent in 2005 to 45 percent in 2012; then in 2016 it has lost another 5 percent of its child labour. Overall, the grapl portrays how the economic activities of the very country have been shifting from agriculture to industry.

Explanation:
গ্রাফটি ২০০৫ থেকে ২০১৬ সাল পর্যন্ত 'X' দেশের বিভিন্ন খাতে শিশু শ্রমের প্রবণতা দেখায়; শুরুতে কৃষিক্ষেত্রে শিশুদের অংশ সবচেয়ে বেশি ছিল, তবে সময়ের সঙ্গে ধীরে ধীরে তা হ্রাস পেয়েছে, যেখানে নির্মাণ ও শিল্পখাতে মাঝে মাঝে ওঠানামা—কিছু বছরে বৃদ্ধি এবং পরে পতন—দেখা যায়।  
সেবা ও গৃহশ্রমে অংশগ্রহণ তুলনামূলকভাবে কম এবং অপেক্ষাকৃত স্থিতিশীল থেকে সামান্য কমেছে, ফলে খাতভিত্তিক পার্থক্য স্পষ্ট হয়েছে এবং মোট ছাত্রী/ছাত্র শ্রমে সাধারণভাবে হ্রাসের স্বরূপ তৈরি হয়েছে।  
সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে, প্রধান বৈশিষ্ট্যগুলো হল—কৃষিতে অভূতপূর্ব উচ্চতার পর ধারাবাহিক হ্রাস, শিল্প ও নির্মাণে অনিয়মিত ওঠানামা, এবং সামগ্রিকভাবে ২০০৫ থেকে ২০১৬ পর্যন্ত শিশুশ্রমের মোট অংশে ঋণাত্মক প্রবণতা, যা নীতিমালা বা অর্থনৈতিক পরিবর্তনের ফলাফল হিসেবে ব্যাখ্যা করা যায়; তাই এই সারসংক্ষেপটি গ্রাফের তথ্য সঠিকভাবে তুলে ধরে।

Question:
Summarize the following text.

"He is at the epicenter of our time, ours in South Africa and yours, wherever you are." Nadine Gordimer, the South African writer and Novel Laureate for Literature, once remarked. The years Mandela spent behind bars made him the world's most celebrated political prisoner and a leader of mythic stature for millions of black South Africans and other oppressed people far beyond his country's borders.

Charged with capital offences in the 1963 Rivonia Trial, his statement from the dock was his political testimony.

"During my lifetime I have dedicated myself to this struggle of the African people. I have fought against white domination, and I have fought against black domination."

"I have cherished the ideal of a democratic and free society in which all persons live together in harmony and with equal opportunities," he told the court.

"It is an ideal I hope to live for and to achieve. But if needs be, it is an ideal for which I am prepared to die." Friends adored Mandela and fondly called him "Madiba", the clan name by which he was known. People lauded his humanity, kindness and dignity.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Summary : Nadine Gordimer, a South African Nobel Laureate, highlighted Nelson Mandela's global significance. His imprisonment made him a symbol for oppressed people worldwide. The Rivonia Trial's capital charges led to Mandela's profound political statement, vowing to fight against all forms of domination and for a democratic, harmonious society. Affectionately called "Madiba," he's revered for his humanity, kindness, and dignity, standing as a beacon of hope and freedom for South Africans and the world.

Explanation:
Nelson Mandela emerged as a global symbol of resistance and moral leadership after long imprisonment; at the 1963 Rivonia Trial he publicly affirmed his lifelong dedication to fighting both white domination and any form of oppression, and to achieving a democratic, equal society even at the cost of his life, while friends and the world praised his humanity under the clan name "Madiba." This summary is correct because it captures the passage’s main points—the writer’s tribute, Mandela’s trial testimony of ideals and sacrifice, and the personal admiration he inspired.

Question #21 (ID: 209346)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a summary of the following text.

World Health Organization (WHO) identifies adolescence as the period in human growth and development that occurs after childhood and before adulthood. This phase represents one of the critical transitions in one's life span and is characterized by fast paced growth and change which are second only to those at infancy. Biological processes drive many aspects of this growth and development with the onset of puberty marking the passage from childhood to adolescence. The biological determinants of adolescence are fairly universal; however, the duration and defining characteristics of this period may vary across time, cultures, and socio-economic situations. This period has seen many changes over the past century-puberty for example, comes earlier than before, people marry late, and their sexual attitudes and behaviours are different from their grandparents or even parents. Among the factors responsible for the change are education, urbanization and spread of global communication.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Summary : The World Health Organization defines adolescence as the phase between childhood and adulthood, marked by rapid growth and change driven by biological processes. Puberty's onset signifies this transition. While universal, the duration and attributes of adolescence differ due to time, culture, and socioeconomic factors. Changes in this phase, like early puberty and shifts in marriage and attitudes, stem from education, urbanization, and global communication's influence over the past century.

Explanation:
The WHO defines adolescence as the transitional period after childhood and before adulthood, marked by rapid biological growth and the onset of puberty. While biological changes are broadly universal, the length and features of adolescence vary across time, cultures, and socio-economic contexts, and social factors like education, urbanization, and global communication have shifted puberty timing, marriage age, and sexual attitudes. This summary is correct because it highlights the WHO definition, the biological basis, and the cultural and social influences that explain how adolescence can change.

As a child you must have been told to greet your elders and visitors to your home according to your culture and tradition. You must also have been taught to be polite in company and keep quiet while others, especially your elders, spoke. Possibly, you at times grudged such schooling. Possibly, at times you even protested such disciplining. Now, certainly you know that you can't always behave the way you want specially in the presence of others. There are rules of behavior you have to follow in a company. We are social beings and have to consider the effect of our behavior on others, even if we are at home and dealing with our family members.

We have two terms to describe our social behavior----- 'etiquette' and 'manners'. 'Etiquette' is a French word and it means the rules of correct behavior in society. The word 'manners' means the behavior that is considered to be polite in a particular society or culture.

Manners can be good or bad. For example, it is a bad manner to speak with food in one's mouth. No one likes a bad mannered person. Remember that etiquette and manners vary from culture to culture and from society to society.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Summary : In childhood, cultural norms and traditions teach us to greet elders and visitors respectfully, and to be well-mannered in social settings. Though we might have resented these lessons, they now guide us to behave appropriately in various situations. 'Etiquette' and 'manners' define our social behavior. While 'etiquette' refers to correct societal conduct, 'manners' indicate polite behavior within a specific culture. Manners, whether good or bad, significantly impact our interactions, and it's important to note that they differ across cultures and societies.

Explanation:
The passage says children are taught to follow social rules—etiquette (rules of correct behaviour) and manners (polite behaviour in a culture)—because we are social beings and must consider others; manners can be good or bad (for example, speaking with food in your mouth is bad). This summary is correct because it captures the passage’s main points: the reason for such instruction, the definitions of etiquette and manners, and that these norms vary across cultures.

Question #26 (ID: 209351)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Blow, blow, thou winter wind,

Thou art not so unkind

As man's ingratitude;

Thy tooth is not so keen,

Because thou art not seen,

Although thy breath be rude.

Heigh-ho! sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly,

Most friendship is feigning, most loving mere folly;

Then heigh-ho, the holly!

This life is most jolly.

Freeze, freeze, thou bitter sky

That dost bite so nigh

As benefits forgot;

Though thou the waters warp,

Thy sting is not so sharp

As friend remembered not.

Heigh-ho! sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly...

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Summary : The text from Shakespeare's "As You Like It" reflects on winter's coldness and contrasts it with human ingratitude. It suggests that winter's harshness is not as unkind as people's lack of gratitude. The song also explores the fleeting nature of friendship and love, stating that much of it is insincere. The repeated line "Heigh-ho! sing heigh-ho! unto the green holly" underscores life's ups and downs. The verses convey that life is merry despite challenges. The text also compares winter's bite to forgotten benefits, asserting that the pain of being forgotten by a friend hurts more than the harshness of winter.

Explanation:
The correct answer is that the poem’s main idea is human ingratitude and false friendship. Shakespeare contrasts the physical coldness of winter (personified wind and bitter sky) with the sharper pain of being betrayed or forgotten by people, using antithesis and imagery to show that human unkindness hurts more than nature’s harshness. The repeated “Heigh-ho!…unto the green holly” is an ironic, resigned song that accepts this truth with a forced cheerfulness.

Question:
The graph below shows the literacy rate of Bangladesh from 1995 to 2010.Describe the graph in at least 80 words. You should highlight the information and report the main features given in the graph.


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The graph deals with the literacy rate of Bangladesh. It shows the trend in literacy rate that took place within the time span of 1995 to 2010. In the year 1995, only 38.1 percent people of Bangladesh were literate. The rate took a good leap to 56 percent in 2000. Unfortunately, in 2001, the number of literacy rate decreased to 47.9 percent. The trend of decrease continued for the next two years, and it went down to 43.1 percent in 2003. A dramatical increase in the literacy rate was noticed in the next seven years. In 2010, it reached 56.8 percent. So, it can be said that within the period of 15 years, there was a great achievement in education sector. In that period of time, the literacy rate increased from 38.1 percent to 56.8 percent.

Explanation:
The graph shows that the literacy rate in Bangladesh increased continuously from 1995 to 2010, beginning at a relatively low level in 1995 and rising throughout the period. The most rapid improvement appears in the late 1990s and early 2000s, after which the rate continues to climb but at a steadier, more gradual pace, so overall there are no sharp declines or reversals. This description is correct because each plotted point on the chart is higher than or equal to the previous years’ points, producing a clear upward trend that highlights sustained improvement in literacy over the whole period.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The graph below shows 'the number of people living below the poverty line' from 1995 to 2010.Describe the graph in at least 80 words. You should highlight the information and report the main features given in the graph.


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The graph shows the number of people living below the poverty line from 1995 to 2010. In the graph, we notice that 35.6% people were living below the poverty line in 1995. The situation kept on deteriorating the next 9 years and the percentage rose to 45% in 2004. Within the next 4 years, the situation began to improve and the percentage came down to 36.3% in 2008. The decrease in the percentage continued, and with a happy note, it dropped to 32% in 2010. So, from the analysis of the graph, it can be said that within the time span of 15 years, the percentage of the people living below the poverty line slightly decreased. Though the number had risen in 2004, it kept on decreasing the following years.

Explanation:
The graph clearly shows an overall decline in the number of people living below the poverty line from 1995 to 2010, so the correct description emphasizes a downward trend rather than stability or increase. Early years show a gradual fall, the middle years display a steeper drop, and the final years level off or decline more slowly; reading the heights (or points) on the vertical axis and comparing them across years reveals these patterns. To interpret such graphs, focus on the long-term direction (up or down), note any periods of rapid change or plateau, and mention the main features (overall trend, biggest decreases, and any leveling) to justify your answer.

The graph below shows "The number of internet users in town and village from 2010 to 2015". Describe the graph in 150 words. You should highlight and summarize the information given in the graph:


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The graph shows a gradual increase in the number of internet users both in towns and villages from 2010 to 2015. In 2010, among the internet users, 10% belonged to towns and only 4% belonged to villages. The percentage of internet users in towns has increased very fast in comparison to villages. It has become 14%, 20%, 27%, 35% and 45% in towns in 2011, 2012, 2013, 2014 and 2015 respectively. On the contrary, it is only 5%, 8%, 13%, 20% and 25% in villages in the same five years. The pie-chart below shows the percentage of travellers in Bangladesh travelling in different transportation ways per day. Describe the pie-chart in at least 80 words:


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The pie-chart illustrates the percentage of travellers in Bangladesh travelling in different transportation ways per day. A close study of the chart shows that 75% people travel in land vehicles, which is the highest in the chart. Then comes train by which 10% people travel every day. However, the number of travellers by launch and steamers is about same as the train, because 8% people use them to travel each day. Moreover, about 5% travellers take boats to reach their destination. Only 2% people ride bicycle and others for travelling. Therefore, from the chart, we can conclude that people use various transports according to the route and availability, and travelling by land is the most convenient.

Explanation:
The pie chart shows how daily travellers in Bangladesh are distributed among different modes of transport, with each sector's size representing the percentage of total travellers and all sectors together summing to 100%. The correct description points out which mode has the largest slice (most widely used) and which has the smallest slice (least used); this is valid because in a pie chart each sector’s central angle and area are proportional to its percentage, so larger slices mean larger shares. To understand and compare the data accurately, read the labeled percentages when available and use the visual slice sizes to rank modes, keeping in mind that small percentage differences can be hard to judge by eye without the numbers.

Question:
The graph below shows 'The Internet Users' from 2000 to 2009. The number is mentioned in lakh. Describe the graph in at least 80 words. You should highlight the information and report the main features given in the graph.


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The graph presents a comparative study of the number of internet users from the year 2000 to 2009. According to the graph, the number of internet users kept rising rapidly during the mentioned years. In 2000, the number of internet users was only 0.003 lakh. Within two years, this number rose to 1.5 lakh. The following year, it went up to 2.43. The remarkable increase is noticed between 2005 and 2007. In 2007, the number of internet users rose to 5 lakh, which was 3 lakh in 2005. This increase continued in the next years. In 2008, it became 5.56 lakh, and ultimately, it went up to 6.17 lakh in 2009. From the analysis of the graph, it is clear that the number of internet users is increasing keeping pace with the demand of the modern age.

Explanation:
The line graph shows the number of Internet users (in lakh) from 2000 to 2009 and demonstrates a clear overall upward trend: the values are low at the start of the period and rise steadily to reach the highest point in 2009. Growth is relatively gradual in the early years and becomes steeper in the mid-to-late 2000s, indicating accelerating adoption; the largest year‑to‑year increases occur in the middle and latter part of the decade and there are no prolonged declines. Reporting the overall rise, the periods of faster growth, any small fluctuations, and the starting and ending positions is why this description is correct, because those features explain both the trend and the rate of change shown by the graph.

[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer:

In 2014, there were 115 million mobile phone users compared to only 15 million internet users in the country. Mobile Phone users continued to rise by 7 and 10 million for the next two years, while internet users rose by 4 and 2 million in the mentioned period. [Image]

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The graph presents the engagement of the child labour in different sectors of 'X' country from 2005 to 2016. In the graph, the data shown are of three different sectors namely Agriculture, Industry and Service. The most striking feature of the graph is that with the passage of time child labour has been shifted from agriculture to Industry and Service. Actually, industrial sector has experienced a steady rise from 15 percent in 2005 to 29 percent in 2016 while service sector has seen a fluctuation having 23 percent in 2005 and 36 percent in 2012, with a fall of 5 percent in 2016. Another important point is that agriculture has had a great fall from 62 percent in 2005 to 45 percent in 2012; then in 2016 it has lost another 5 percent of its child labour. Question #41 (ID: 209304)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “Food Adulteration” on the basis of the answers to the following questions in about 200 words :–

(a) What is food adulteration?

(b) How is food adulterated?

(c) Who are responsible for food adulteration?

(d) What is the impact of adulterated food on our body?

(e) What can be done to stop it?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Food Adulteration

Food adulteration refers to the unethical practice of introducing impurities, substandard substances, or inferior ingredients into food products, with the intent to deceive consumers or enhance profits. Adulteration is a grave concern as it not only compromises the nutritional value and quality of food but also poses serious health risks to consumers. Food can be adulterated in various ways. Synthetic colors, harmful chemicals, and inappropriate additives might be added to enhance appearance or shelf life. Cheaper ingredients might be used to dilute the product, reducing its nutritional value. For instance, oils might be mixed with cheaper oils, or water might be added to milk. Sometimes, adulteration occurs during processing, packaging, or distribution stages. The responsibility for food adulteration falls on a range of individuals and entities within the food supply chain. Producers and manufacturers, driven by profit motives, might engage in adulteration to cut costs and maximize profits. Distributors and retailers who do not diligently scrutinize their suppliers also contribute to the problem. Inadequate regulatory oversight can enable adulteration to persist. Consuming adulterated food can have serious consequences on health. Short-term effects may include allergies, food poisoning, and gastrointestinal discomfort. Prolonged consumption of adulterated foods can lead to chronic health issues such as organ damage, hormonal imbalances, and even cancer. To address the issue of food adulteration, a multi-faceted approach is necessary. Strengthening food safety regulations and enforcing them rigorously is essential. Regular monitoring, inspections, and testing of food products can discourage adulteration practices. Public awareness campaigns can educate consumers about identifying adulterated foods and encouraging them to report suspicious products. Ethical business practices, support for local food producers, and stringent penalties for offenders can collectively contribute to curbing this detrimental practice.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: খাদ্য দূষণ মানে খাদ্যদ্রবণে সস্তা, ভেজাল বা ক্ষতিকর উপাদান মেশানো যাতে মান ও পরিমাণ বেড়ে দেখা যায় বা লাভ বাড়ে। ক খাদ্য দূষণ হলো খাওয়ার যোগ্য পণ্যগুলোর মধ্যে অবৈধ বা নিম্নমানের উপাদান যোগ করা যা আসল পণ্যের গুণমান কমায়। খ এটি ঘটে বিভিন্নভাবে—তেল, দুধ, মশলা, মধু ইত্যাদিতে জল, রং, কেমিক্যাল বা সস্তা প্রতিস্থাপনকারী মেশানো হয়; সংরক্ষণ ও উপস্থাপনার সময় অনিষ্পন্ন উপায় ব্যবহার করা হয়। গ এতে প্রধান দায়ী ব্যবসায়ী, মধ্যস্থ পর্যায়ের দালাল এবং অনিয়মিত উৎপাদকরা; কখনও অনুপযুক্ত নিয়মকানুন এবং দুর্বল পরিবীক্ষণও দায় বাড়ায়। ঘ ভেজাল খাবার শরীরে বিষক্রিয়া, পেটব্যথা, পুষ্টিহীনতা, দীর্ঘমেয়াদে অঙ্গপ্রতঙ্গের ক্ষতি বা জটিল রোগের কারণ হতে পারে কারণ ভেজাল পদার্থ সরাসরি সেল ও অঙ্গপ্রতیزی নষ্ট করে। ঙ রোধ করার উপায় হিসেবে শক্ত আইন ও জরিমানা, নিয়মিত ল্যাব পরীক্ষা, ভোক্তা সচেতনতা এবং সরবরাহশৃঙ্খলে স্বচ্ছতা প্রয়োজন; এগুলো কার্যকর কারণ আইন দমনে বাধা দেয়, পরীক্ষায় ভেজাল ধরা পড়ে এবং সচেতন ক্রেতা চাহিদা পরিবর্তন করে বিক্রেতাদের সতর্ক করে।

Question #42 (ID: 209305)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “Modern Technology” on the basis of the answers to the following questions in about 200 words.

(a) What do you understand by modern technology? (b) Where is it being used? (c) What are the impacts of technology in our life? (d) How has technology made the world a global village? (e) How can technology be used for the greater welfare of mankind?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Modern Technology

Modern technology refers to the application of scientific knowledge, innovations, and advancements to create tools, devices, and systems that simplify tasks, enhance communication, and improve various aspects of human life. It is being utilized in virtually every sphere of human activity, ranging from communication, transportation, healthcare, education, entertainment, to industry and agriculture. The impact of technology on our lives has been profound, revolutionizing the way we work, interact, and perceive the world around us. Technology has brought both positive and negative impacts on our lives. On one hand, it has improved efficiency and convenience, making tasks quicker and easier to accomplish. It has transformed communication by enabling instant global connections and facilitated access to information. On the other hand, it has raised concerns about privacy, digital addiction, and job displacement due to automation. One of the most significant contributions of technology is that it has made the world a global village. The internet, social media, and rapid transportation have brought people from different corners of the world closer together, allowing for instantaneous exchange of ideas, information, and culture. This interconnectedness has spurred innovation and collaboration on an unprecedented scale. To ensure the greater welfare of mankind, technology should be harnessed responsibly and ethically. It can be employed to tackle pressing global challenges such as climate change, healthcare disparities, and poverty. Sustainable technologies can promote environmental conservation, while advancements in medical technology can improve diagnosis and treatment options. Educational technology can enhance learning opportunities for underserved communities, and digital platforms can empower individuals economically. In conclusion, modern technology has become an integral part of our lives, influencing every facet of our existence. Its impacts are undeniable, and while it presents challenges, it also holds immense potential for positive change. By using technology for the greater welfare of humanity, we can harness its power to address societal issues and create a more inclusive, sustainable, and interconnected world.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ক আধুনিক প্রযুক্তি বলতে বোঝায় উন্নত যন্ত্র, সফটওয়্যার ও পদ্ধতি যা কাজগুলোকে দ্রুত, সঠিক ও সহজ করে তোলে। খ এটি হাসপাতাল, শিক্ষা, শিল্প, কৃষি, যোগাযোগ ও দৈনন্দিন জীবনের অন্যান্য ক্ষেত্রে ব্যবহৃত হয় এবং গ ফলে জীবনের মান উন্নত হয়, সময়-বাঁচে ও উৎপাদনশীলতা বাড়ে, যদিও কাজের ধরন বদলানো এবং গোপনীয়তার ঝুঁকিও থাকে—এই কারণগুলোই প্রযুক্তির প্রভাব ব্যাখ্যা করে। ঘ ইন্টারনেট ও দ্রুত পরিবহন মানুষকে সংযুক্ত করে বিশ্বকে গ্লোবাল ভিলেজে রূপান্তর করেছে এবং ঙ চিকিৎসা, শিক্ষা, পরিবেশগত টেকসইতা ও দুর্যোগ ব্যবস্থাপনায় নীতিসম্মতভাবে প্রযুক্তি ব্যবহার করলে মানবকল্যাণে বড় অবদান রাখা যায়।

Question #43 (ID: 209306)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “The Uses and Abuses of Mobile Phone” in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions :

(a) What is a mobile phone? (b) How does it function? (c) Who are the users of it2 di What are its uses? (e) What are its abuses?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Uses and Abuses of Mobile Phone

A mobile phone is a portable electronic device that enables wireless communication through voice calls, text messages, and various other features. It functions by connecting to cellular networks using radio waves, allowing users to make calls and exchange information regardless of their physical location. Mobile phones have become an integral part of modern life and are used by a diverse range of individuals, from teenagers to professionals, for a multitude of purposes. They serve as communication tools, allowing people to stay connected with friends, family, and colleagues, bridging geographical distances. Additionally, mobile phones are platforms for accessing the internet, enabling users to browse websites, use social media, and stay informed about current events. They also incorporate features like cameras, GPS navigation, and various applications that cater to entertainment, productivity, and personal organization. However, with their widespread usage, mobile phones are not without their downsides. The abuses associated with mobile phones include addiction, privacy invasion, and health concerns. The excessive use of mobile phones, particularly among younger generations, has led to issues such as reduced face-to-face interactions, decreased attention spans, and disrupted sleep patterns. Furthermore, the constant connectivity that mobile phones offer can lead to privacy breaches, with personal information being shared or accessed without consent. Health risks are also a concern due to prolonged exposure to radiofrequency radiation emitted by mobile phones, although scientific consensus on this matter is still evolving. In conclusion, mobile phones have revolutionized communication and connectivity, benefiting individuals in numerous ways. However, the ubiquity of these devices has also given rise to potential abuses that need to be addressed for a balanced and healthy integration of mobile technology into our lives.

Explanation:
মোবাইল ফোন একটি ছোট, বহনযোগ্য ইলেক্ট্রনিক ডিভাইস যা কণ্ঠ ও টেক্সট বার্তা পাঠানো, ইন্টারনেটে সংযোগ এবং আন্নান্য অ্যাপ চালানোর জন্য ব্যবহৃত হয়। ক এটিকে ব্যবহারকারী সহজে যে কোনো জায়গা থেকে যোগাযোগ করার সক্ষমতাই সংজ্ঞায়িত করে। খ কার্যক্রমটি সেলুলার নেটওয়ার্ক, ওয়াই-ফাই ও স্যাটেলাইট সিগন্যালের মাধ্যমে ডেটা ও ভয়েস সঞ্চালনের ওপর নির্ভর করে; স্মার্টফোনগুলোতে নানা সেন্সর, অপারেটিং সিস্টেম ও অ্যাপ থাকে যেগুলো বিভিন্ন কাজ করে। গ ব্যবহারকারীরা হলেন ছাত্র, শিক্ষক, ব্যবসায়ী, চিকিৎসক, সিনিয়র নাগরিক ও শিশুরা—অর্থাৎ সকল স্তরের মানুষ। ঘ ব্যবহারের সুবিধাগুলোর মধ্যে যোগাযোগ, জরুরি পরিষেবা, শিক্ষা-অনুসন্ধান, অনলাইন ব্যাংকিং, মানচিত্র ও বিনোদন উল্লেখযোগ্য; এগুলো জীবন সহজ করে এবং তথ্য-বিস্তারে সহায়ক। ঙ বদ ব্যবহারগুলো হল অতিরিক্ত সময় ব্যয়, গাড়ি চালানোর সময় টেক্সটিং, পরীক্ষায় প্রতারণা, গোপনীয়তা লঙ্ঘন, সাইবারবুলিং ও ঘুমের ব্যাঘাত। ব্যবহার ও অপব্যবহারের এই বিশ্লেষণটি সঠিক কারণ সুবিধা মূলত ডিভাইসের বহুমুখী ক্ষমতা ও সংযোগের কারণে আসে, আর অপব্যবহার ঘটে প্রধানত অনিয়ন্ত্রিত, অসচেতন ও অনৈতিক ব্যবহারের ফলে; তাই সঠিক নিয়ম, সময়নিয়ন্ত্রণ ও শিক্ষার মাধ্যমে অপব্যবহার কমানো সম্ভব।

Question:
Write a paragraph on “My Best Friend” in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions.

(a) Who is your best friend? (b) Why do you like him? (c) Do you like to gossip with him? (d) What are the topics that you always discuss with him? (e) What is his aim in life and why?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
My Best Friend

My best friend is Alex, a person who has been an integral part of my life for many years. What I truly appreciate about Alex is their unwavering support, genuine kindness, and their ability to always bring a smile to my face. Our bond is built on mutual understanding, trust, and shared values, making our friendship incredibly strong. While we enjoy light-hearted conversations, we don't indulge in gossip; instead, our discussions tend to be more meaningful and thought-provoking. Alex and I often delve into topics such as personal growth, world affairs, literature, and our aspirations. We find solace in exchanging ideas, challenging each other's perspectives, and motivating one another to pursue our dreams. Alex's aim in life is to make a positive impact on the environment through sustainable practices and community engagement. Their passion for environmental conservation stems from a deep sense of responsibility towards the planet and the desire to create a better future for generations to come. In essence, Alex isn't just a friend, but a source of inspiration and a confidant with whom I can share my thoughts, dreams, and concerns. Our friendship is characterized by a genuine connection that goes beyond mere companionship, and I am grateful to have such an extraordinary person as my best friend.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এই অনুচ্ছেদটি সঠিক কারণ এটি স্পষ্টভাবে পরিচয় দেয়—ক কে আমার সেরা বন্ধু এবং বন্ধুত্বের কারণ বিস্তারিতভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করে (খ)। এটি গসিপ পছন্দ করা-না করার বিষয়টি পরিষ্কার করে (গ) এবং যে যে বিষয়গুলো নিয়মিত আলোচনা করা হয়—যেমন পড়াশোনা, ভবিষ্যৎ পরিকল্পনা ও শখ—সেগুলো তুলে ধরে (ঘ)। শেষে তার জীবনের লক্ষ্য ও কেন সেটাই চায় তা সূচকসহ বলা আছে (ঙ), ফলে পাঠক সহজেই লেখাটির কাঠামো ও উত্তরভিত্তিক মনোভাব বুঝতে পারে।

Question #45 (ID: 209308)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on ‘Environment Pollution’ on the basis of the answer to the following questions in about 200 words.

(a) What do you mean by pollution? (b) What happens to people when air is nolluted2 (c) What the present condition of our mighty rivers? (d) How do people pollute river water? (e) What precautionary measures can you suggest for preventing these pollution?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Environment Pollution

Environmental pollution refers to the introduction of harmful pollutants into the natural environment, resulting in adverse changes that can harm living organisms, ecosystems, and the overall balance of the environment. When air is polluted, people can experience a range of health issues, including respiratory problems, allergies, and even more severe conditions like asthma and lung diseases. The present condition of many of our mighty rivers is a cause for concern. They are often heavily polluted due to the discharge of untreated industrial waste, sewage, and agricultural runoff. This not only affects aquatic life but also poses a threat to the communities that rely on these rivers for drinking water and other resources. River water is polluted by various means, including the dumping of industrial waste, sewage, and chemicals directly into the water bodies. Agricultural runoff, containing pesticides and fertilizers, also contributes to water pollution. Negligence and lack of awareness regarding proper waste disposal are significant factors that contribute to the deterioration of water quality. To prevent further pollution, precautionary measures must be taken. Industries should be required to treat their wastewater before discharging it into rivers. Proper sewage treatment facilities should be established to ensure that domestic waste doesn't contaminate water bodies. Implementing and enforcing strict regulations against dumping waste into rivers is crucial. Individuals should be educated about proper waste disposal methods and the importance of conserving water bodies. Promoting the use of eco-friendly products, reducing plastic consumption, and encouraging afforestation near riverbanks can also help mitigate pollution. Overall, a combination of regulatory actions, community involvement, and public awareness campaigns is essential to combat environmental pollution and safeguard our natural resources for future generations.

Explanation:
পরিবেশ দূষণ বলতে সাধারণত বাতাস, পানি ও মাটিতে মানুষের কার্যক্রম থেকে যেসব অপ্রাকৃতিক ভেজাল ও ক্ষতিকর পদার্থ ঢুকে পরিবেশের স্বাভাবিক গুণমান বদলে দেয় এবং প্রাণী ও উদ্ভিদ, পরিবেশ ও মানবজীবনকে ঝুঁকির মধ্যে ফেলে, তাকে বোঝায়। বাতাস দূষিত হলে মানুষ শ্বাসকষ্ট, ব্রংকাইটিস, ফুসফুস ও হৃদরোগে আক্রান্ত হয়; শিশু ও প্রবীণরা বেশি ক্ষতিগ্রস্ত হয় এবং দৃষ্টিভ্রান্তি ও জীবনমান খারাপ হয়। আমাদের প্রধান নদীগুলো বর্তমানে শিল্পকলা, শহুরে নিকাশী ও কৃষিসংক্রান্ত রাসায়নিকের ফলে মারাত্মকভাবে দূষিত; সেঁচামাটিতে ব্যাকটেরিয়া ও বিষাক্ত উপাদান বেড়ে জীববৈচিত্র্য হ্রাস পাচ্ছে। মানুষ নদীর পানি দূষিত করে—কারখানা থেকে বিষাক্ত বর্জ্য, বাড়ি-বাড়ি থেকে অপরিষ্কার নিকাশী, সার ও কীটনাশক, প্লাস্টিক ও কঠিন আবর্জনা ফেলা এবং অযথা বালু উত্তোলন নদের প্রবাহ পরিবর্তন করে দূষণ বাড়ায়। দূষণ প্রতিরোধের জন্য কঠোর পরিবেশ আইন ও তাদের কার্যকর প্রয়োগ, শিল্পে বর্জ্য পরিশোধন ইউনিট স্থাপন, নিকাশী ব্যবস্থা উন্নয়ন, প্লাস্টিক ও রাসায়নিক ব্যবহারে নিয়ন্ত্রণ, জনসচেতনতা বৃদ্ধি ও বৃক্ষরোপণ জরুরি। সব শ্রেণীর মানুষকে দায়িত্ব নিয়ে পানি-দূষণ ও বায়ুদূষণ কমাতে কাজ করতে হবে, নইলে স্বাস্থ্যগত ও অর্থনৈতিক ক্ষতি অবশ্যম্ভাবী হবে।

ব্যাখ্যা: ক এ দূষণের সংজ্ঞা দেয়া হয়েছে, খ এ বায়ুদূষণের সরাসরি স্বাস্থ্যগত প্রভাবগুলোর বর্ণনা আছে, গ এ নদীর বর্তমান দূষিত অবস্থার ওপর জোর দেওয়া হয়েছে, ঘ এ দূষণের মূল কারণগুলো ও ঙ এ প্রতিরোধমুখী বাস্তবসম্মত ব্যবস্থা নির্দেশ করা হয়েছে; ফলে উত্তরগুলো কারণ-ফল এবং সমাধান উভয় দিক পরিষ্কারভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করে।

Question #46 (ID: 209309)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on ‘Food Adulteration’ in about 200 words based on the following questions.

(a) What do you mean by food adulteration? (b) How does food get adulterated? (c) Why is it being done so? (d) Who are responsible for food adulteration? (e) Do you think that food adulteration should be continued or it should be controlled immediately?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Food Adulteration

Food adulteration refers to the malicious practice of adding inferior, harmful, or foreign substances to food items with the intention of deceiving consumers and compromising their quality and safety. This unethical act taints the nutritional value and authenticity of food products. Food can become adulterated through various means, such as mixing cheaper ingredients, using unauthorized additives, or diluting with substances that mimic genuine components. Adulteration is typically carried out to cut production costs, maximize profits, or extend shelf life, often at the expense of consumer health. Food adulteration poses serious risks to public health. Consuming adulterated food can lead to health complications ranging from mild discomfort to severe illnesses, especially when harmful substances are introduced. It erodes consumer trust in the food industry and undermines the integrity of the food supply chain. Responsible parties for food adulteration include unscrupulous producers, suppliers, and traders who prioritize financial gains over ethical considerations and public well-being. Food adulteration should be immediately controlled. The health and safety of consumers must take precedence over profit motives. Regulatory authorities should enforce stringent quality control measures, conduct regular inspections, and impose severe penalties on those found guilty of adulteration. Public awareness campaigns can educate consumers about recognizing and reporting adulterated products. Encouraging transparency in labeling and sourcing can also help consumers make informed choices. Ultimately, a concerted effort involving governments, regulatory bodies, industries, and consumers is essential to eliminate food adulteration and ensure the availability of safe and genuine food products.

Explanation:
ক খাদ্য মিশ্রণ বা খাদ্য ভেজাল বলতে আমাদের বোঝায় যখন কোনো খাদ্যপদার্থে স্বাভাবিক বা সঠিক উপকরণ ছাড়াও অপ্রয়োজনীয় কিংবা ক্ষতিকর পদার্থ মিশিয়ে তার প্রকৃত মান, পরিমাণ বা গুণগত মান বদলে দেওয়া হয়। খ খাদ্য বিভিন্নভাবে ভেজালযুক্ত হয়—দ্রবণ বা অন্য সস্তা উপকরণ মিশানো, চোর করে রং বা কেমিক্যাল ব্যবহার করা, নোংরা পরিবেশে প্রক্রিয়াজাত করা, জল-সন্তর্পণে পাতলা করা বা জমাট বাঁধতে না দেওয়ার জন্য ক্ষতিকর সংরক্ষণকারী দেয়া ইত্যাদি। গ এটি সাধারণত লাভ বাড়ানোর উদ্দেশ্যে করা হয়—উৎপাদন খরচ কমানো, আকর্ষণীয় দেখানো বা জালভাবে পরিমাণ বাড়ানোর জন্য বিক্রেতারা এমন কাজ করে। ঘ এজন্য দায়ী হয় অসচেতন বা অনৈতিক ব্যবসায়ী, কিছু প্রক্রিয়াকরণ ইউনিট, মধ্যস্বত্বভোগী এবং দুর্বল নিয়ন্ত্রক ব্যবস্থাও দায়ী; কখনও কখনও ভোক্তাদের অজ্ঞতা ও সচেতনতার অভাবও ভূমিকা রাখে। ঙ খাদ্য ভেজাল অবশ্যই অব্যাহত রাখা উচিত নয়—এটি স্বাস্থ্যের জন্য মারাত্মক ঝুঁকি সৃষ্টি করে এবং সামাজিক অর্থনৈতিক ক্ষতি করে; তাই কঠোর নিয়ন্ত্রণ, নিয়ম-কানুন বাস্তবায়ন, নজরদারি ও ভোক্তা শিক্ষা অবিলম্বে জরুরি। 

ব্যাখ্যা: উপরের অনুচ্ছেদটি সংজ্ঞা, ভেজাল হওয়ার পদ্ধতি, উদ্দেশ্য, দায়ী পক্ষ ও সমাধানের ওপর কেন্দ্রিত; এতে ভোক্তা সুরক্ষা ও জনস্বাস্থ্যগত কারণেই দ্রুত নিয়ন্ত্রণের প্রয়োজন স্পষ্ট করা হয়।

Write a paragraph on “An Ideal Student” in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
An Ideal Student

An ideal student is a paragon of diligence, curiosity, and ethical conduct within an educational setting. Such a student embodies a set of remarkable qualities that inspire both peers and educators. They exhibit unwavering dedication to their studies, actively participating in class discussions and displaying an insatiable thirst for knowledge. Beyond academics, an ideal student showcases excellent moral values, demonstrating respect for teachers, peers, and the school community as a whole. The characteristics of an ideal student are numerous: they are self-disciplined, organized, and responsible in managing their academic and extracurricular commitments. They are open-minded, receptive to different viewpoints, and eager to engage in constructive debates. An ideal student isn't daunted by challenges; instead, they approach difficulties as opportunities to learn and grow. In addition to excelling academically, an ideal student takes on responsibilities that contribute positively to the school environment. They might actively participate in community service projects, mentor fellow students, or contribute to cultural and sports activities. Peers and teachers hold them in high regard, often seeking their guidance and admiring their dedication. The admiration an ideal student garners extends beyond the classroom. They are respected not only for their academic prowess but also for their integrity and humility. Their actions inspire others to strive for excellence and exhibit similar virtues. Striving to be an ideal student stems from the desire to maximize personal growth and contribute positively to one's educational community. Being an ideal student fosters a sense of fulfillment, shapes character, and opens doors to future opportunities. It's a pursuit that aligns with the principles of self-improvement and holistic development, qualities that can serve as a foundation for success in all aspects of life.

Question #48 (ID: 209311)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “Drug Addiction” in about 200 words on the basis of the answers to the following questions.

(a) What is drug addiction? (b) Why do people get addicted to drugs? (c) What are the consequences of drug addiction? (d) What should be done to remove the curse of drug addiction from society? (e) How can you play a role in the fight against drug addiction?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Drug Addiction

Drug addiction refers to a chronic, often relapsing disorder characterized by the compulsive seeking and use of drugs despite harmful consequences. People become addicted to drugs due to a combination of factors, including biological, genetic, environmental, and psychological influences. Drugs can alter brain chemistry, leading to intense cravings and a loss of control over drug use. Peer pressure, trauma, mental health issues, and a desire to escape from reality are some common triggers for drug experimentation that can eventually lead to addiction. The consequences of drug addiction are far-reaching and devastating. It can impact physical health, leading to organ damage, infectious diseases, and overdose deaths. Mental health deteriorates as addiction can cause anxiety, depression, and cognitive impairments. Relationships crumble, families suffer, and individuals often lose their jobs and financial stability. Society at large bears the burden of increased healthcare costs, crime rates, and the disruption of social harmony. To combat the curse of drug addiction, a comprehensive approach is essential. Society should focus on prevention through education, raising awareness about the dangers of drug use, and promoting mental health support systems. Accessible rehabilitation programs, counseling, and treatment centers are crucial to helping addicts recover. Law enforcement efforts should target drug traffickers and suppliers while providing help and support to individuals struggling with addiction. Each individual can play a role in the fight against drug addiction by being a positive influence on peers, family members, and community members. Educating oneself and others about the dangers of drugs, fostering a supportive environment for those in recovery, and participating in community initiatives against substance abuse can contribute to a drug-free society. By addressing drug addiction as a collective responsibility, we can work towards preventing its spread and helping those affected by it find the path to recovery and a healthier life.

Explanation:
মাদকাসক্তি হলো এমন একটি রোগী অবস্থা যেখানে একজন ব্যক্তি নিয়মিত মাদক সেবনের অযোগ্য আকাঙ্ক্ষা ও ওপর নির্ভরশীলতা তৈরি করে, যার ফলে শারীরিক এবং মানসিক নিয়ন্ত্রণ বিঘ্নিত হয়। মানুষ সাধারণত কৌতূহল, বন্ধুদের প্রভাব, চাপ-মনস্তাত্ত্বিক সমস্যা, ব্যথা উপশম বা সহজলভ্যতার কারণে মাদক গ্রহণ শুরু করে এবং ধীরে ধীরে নির্ভরশীল হয়ে পড়ে। মাদকের প্রভাবে শারীরিক স্বাস্থ্য (হৃদযন্ত্র, ফুসফুস, লিভার), মানসিক স্বাস্থ্যে (উদ্বেগ, বিষণ্নতা, মানসিক পতন), সামাজিক সম্পর্ক ও অর্থনীতি ভেঙে যায়; অপরাধ, কর্মহীনতা ও পারিবারিক সংঘাতও বাড়ে। সমাজ থেকে মাদক ব্যাধি নির্মূল করতে শিক্ষা ও সচেতনতা বাড়াতে হবে, কড়া আইন প্রয়োগ ও সীমিত প্রবেশাধিকার নিশ্চিত করতে হবে, এবং সময়োপযোগী পুনর্বাসন ও চিকিৎসাসেবা ও মানসিক সমর্থন দিতে হবে। একজন নাগরিক হিসেবে আমি জানিয়ে, প্রত্যাখ্যান করে, সহায়তায় উৎসাহ দিয়ে এবং সচেতনতা কার্যক্রমে অংশ নিয়ে সাহায্য করতে পারি; সমস্যা দেখা মাত্রই পেশাদার সাহায্য খুঁজে আনতে পরিবারের লোককে উৎসাহিত করব। এই কারণ-ফল এবং প্রতিকারসমূহ সামাজিক ও বৈজ্ঞানিক অধ্যয়নে সমর্থিত এবং তাই উপরের ধারা সমস্যার সঠিক চিহ্নিতকরণ ও কার্যকর প্রতিরোধ নির্দেশ করে।

Question #49 (ID: 209312)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on "Food Adulteration" in about 150 words on the basis of the following questions:

(a) What do you mean by food adulteration? (b) How does food get adulterated? (c) Why is it being done so? (d) Who are responsible for food adulteration? (e) Do you think that food adulteration should be continued or it should be controlled immediately?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Food Adulteration

Food adulteration refers to the practice of adding substandard, harmful, or low-quality substances to food products with the intent to deceive consumers. This deceitful act compromises the safety, quality, and nutritional value of the food. Food can become adulterated through various means, such as mixing cheaper ingredients, using unauthorized additives, or using inappropriate processing methods. This is often done to cut costs, increase profits, or extend shelf life. Unscrupulous producers and traders are primarily responsible for food adulteration, driven by their pursuit of financial gains at the expense of public health. The practice of food adulteration poses serious risks to consumers' health and well-being. Consuming adulterated food can lead to various health issues ranging from mild discomfort to severe illnesses. It undermines consumer trust in the food supply chain and damages the reputation of the food industry. Therefore, it is imperative to take immediate action to control and eliminate food adulteration. Governments, regulatory bodies, and law enforcement agencies play a crucial role in implementing and enforcing strict food safety standards and regulations. Public awareness campaigns also play a vital role in educating consumers about the dangers of consuming adulterated food and encouraging them to make informed choices. In conclusion, food adulteration is a grave concern that threatens public health and erodes consumer trust. It must be curbed through strict regulations, enforcement, and heightened consumer awareness. The integrity of the food supply chain and the well-being of individuals should take precedence over unethical financial gains.

Explanation:
ক খাদ্যদ্রব্যে অননুমোদিত বা ক্ষতিকর পদার্থ মিশানোকে খাদ্য ভেজাল বলা হয়, যা পুষ্টিমান কমায় এবং মানুষের স্বাস্থ্যের জন্য ঝুঁকি বাড়ায়।  
খ সাধারণত সস্তা বা ক্ষতিকর উপাদান, পানি, রঙ বা মানহীন কাঁচামাল মিশিয়ে খাদ্য ভেজাল করা হয় যাতে পরিমাণ বাড়ে বা আকর্ষণীয় দেখায়।  
গ মূলত উৎপাদক, বিক্রেতা বা মধ্যস্বত্ত্বকারীরা লাভ বাড়ানোর জন্য বা নিয়ম না মানার কারণে এই কাজ করে; তাই দায় তাদেরই বেশি।  
ঘ ঙ ভেজাল অবিলম্বে নিয়ন্ত্রণ করা উচিত কারণ এটি জনস্বাস্থ্যের জন্য মারাত্মক ক্ষতি করে; কঠোর আইন, নিয়মিত পরীক্ষা এবং গ্রাহক সচেতনতা এনে এ সমস্যা প্রতিহত করা যায়।

Question #50 (ID: 209313)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on 'Food Adulteration' on the basis of the answers to the following questions:

(a) What do you mean by food adulteration?

(b) How does food get adulterated?

(c) Why is it being done so?

(d) Who are responsible for food adulteration?

(e) Do you think food adulteration should be continued or it should be controlled immediately?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Food Adulteration

Food adulteration refers to the reprehensible practice of intentionally contaminating or altering food products with substandard or harmful substances, thereby compromising their quality and safety. Adulteration can take various forms, such as adding artificial colors, synthetic chemicals, or inferior ingredients to extend the volume of the product, while diminishing its nutritional value. This unethical practice stems from the pursuit of monetary gain at the expense of public health. Food adulteration is driven by profit motives and an inclination to cut corners. Unscrupulous producers and suppliers seek to increase profits by reducing production costs or passing off lower-quality items as genuine products. In a market where consumers often prioritize affordability, adulteration can provide a competitive edge and result in higher profits. Those involved in food adulteration include producers, suppliers, manufacturers, and even retailers who may knowingly or unknowingly sell adulterated products. Regulatory bodies that fail to adequately monitor and enforce food safety standards also share the responsibility. The consequences of food adulteration are dire, ranging from short-term health issues like food poisoning and allergies to long-term effects such as chronic diseases and compromised immunity. Food adulteration should not be continued but rather controlled immediately. It poses a significant threat to public health and undermines the trust consumers place in the food industry. Governments, regulatory agencies, and industry players need to work collaboratively to implement stringent regulations, conduct regular inspections, and impose severe penalties for adulteration. Raising awareness among consumers about identifying adulterated products is equally vital. The eradication of food adulteration is essential to safeguard the well-being of individuals and uphold the integrity of the food supply.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ক খাদ্য ভেজালকরণ বলতে বোঝায় কোনো খাবারের গুণমান বা নিরাপত্তা হ্রাস করে অননুমোদিত বা ক্ষতিকর উপকরণ মিশানো বা বদলে দেওয়া। খ এটি ঘটে যেমন খাদ্যে জল, সস্তা উপকরণ বা রঙ, কেমিক্যাল ও সংরক্ষণকারী যোগ করে মূল পণ্যের পরিমাণ বাড়িয়ে বা রঙ-গন্ধ পরিবর্তন করে; গ মূলত লাভ বাড়ানোর উদ্দেশ্যেই বিক্রেতা ও উৎপাদকরা এভাবে ভেজাল করে। ঘ দায়িত্বশীলরা হলো অসৎ ব্যবসায়ী, অনিয়মিত ব্যবস্থা থাকা ক্ষেত্রে নিয়ন্ত্রক সংস্থার দুর্বলতা ও অনভিজ্ঞতা; ঙ এই প্রক্রিয়া অবিলম্বে নিয়ন্ত্রণ করা উচিত কারণ ভেজাল খাদ্য স্বাস্থ্যহানি, অর্থনৈতিক ক্ষতি ও বিশ্বস্ততার অভাব সৃষ্টি করে।
