Question #51 (ID: 209314)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on 'Dream' in about 150 words based on the answers to the following questions.

(a) What is a dream? (b) What are the characteristics of a dream? (c) Why do we dream? (d) Do you have any dream in your life? (e) What do you do to fulfil your dream?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Dream

A dream is a complex and ethereal mental experience that occurs during sleep, often involving a sequence of vivid images, emotions, sensations, and ideas. These experiences are characterized by their imaginative and surreal nature, where the laws of reality seem to bend, allowing for situations and scenarios that might be impossible or unlikely in waking life. Dreams can be fleeting and elusive, leaving impressions that range from delightful to unsettling, and they often lack a consistent narrative structure. The exact reasons why we dream remain a subject of ongoing scientific inquiry and debate. Some theories suggest that dreams serve as a means for the brain to process emotions, memories, and experiences, aiding in problem-solving and creative thinking. Others propose that dreams are a result of random neural firings during sleep, and they lack any inherent purpose. Regardless of the specific mechanisms, dreams hold a fascination for their ability to offer insights into our subconscious thoughts and desires. As an AI language model, I don't have personal experiences or consciousness, so I don't have dreams like humans do. However, people often have dreams and aspirations in their lives, ranging from personal achievements to societal changes. To fulfill a dream, individuals often set goals, work diligently, and persevere through challenges. It requires determination, planning, and sometimes adapting strategies along the way. The journey towards fulfilling a dream can be as transformative as the attainment itself, teaching valuable lessons and shaping one's character in the process.

Explanation:
স্বপ্ন বলতে আমরা সাধারণত দুই ধরনের জিনিস বুঝাই: একদিকে ঘুমের সময় মস্তিষ্কে তৈরি হওয়া চিত্র, অনুভূতি ও কল্পনা, আর অন্যদিকে জীবনে অর্জনের জন্য থাকা আকাঙ্ক্ষা বা লক্ষ্য। স্বপ্নের বৈশিষ্ট্য হলো এগুলো জীবন্ত ও আবেগসমৃদ্ধ হতে পারে, অনেক সময় প্রতীকী অর্থ বহন করে এবং দ্রুত বদলে যায়; জীবনীশক্তি যোগায় এবং আমাদের চিন্তা-ভিত্তিক ও সৃজনশীল পক্ষকে উদ্দীপ্ত করে। আমরা কেন স্বপ্ন দেখি—ঘুমের স্বপ্ন মস্তিষ্কের স্মৃতি প্রক্রিয়াকরণ ও আবেগ সামলানোর ফল, আর জীবনের স্বপ্ন আমাদের ভবিষ্যৎ পরিকল্পনা, অনুপ্রেরণা ও প্রচেষ্টার উৎস। আমারও একটি স্বপ্ন আছে—ভালো মানুষ গড়ে তোলার জন্য শিক্ষক হওয়া—এটি পূরণ করতে আমি নিয়মিত পড়াশোনা, দক্ষতা সংগ্রহ, লক্ষ্য নির্ধারণ ও কঠোর পরিশ্রম করছি। এই উত্তরটি সঠিক কারণ ঘুমের ও জীবনের স্বপ্নের মূল বৈশিষ্ট্য ও কাজে লাগার উপায় বৈজ্ঞানিক ও ব্যবহারিকভাবে স্পষ্টভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করে।

Question #52 (ID: 209315)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on 'Price Hike' based on the answers to the following questions:

(a) What is price hike? (b) Why does price of things increase? (c) How do people suffer from price hike? (d) How can we control it? (e) What should we do to stop it?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Price Hike

Price hike, also known as inflation, refers to the sustained increase in the general price level of goods and services within an economy. It occurs when the purchasing power of money decreases, leading to higher costs for consumers. Price hikes are caused by a variety of factors, including increased demand, supply shortages, rising production costs, and changes in monetary policies. The price of things increases due to a combination of factors. Demand-pull inflation happens when consumer demand outpaces supply, driving prices up. Cost-push inflation occurs when production costs, like raw materials or labor, rise, causing businesses to pass on those costs to consumers. Changes in the money supply, such as excessive printing of currency, can also contribute to inflation. People suffer from price hikes in several ways. It erodes the value of their income, making it harder to afford basic necessities. Fixed-income individuals, like retirees, face difficulties as their purchasing power diminishes. Businesses might struggle to maintain profit margins, leading to layoffs and reduced economic growth. High inflation can disrupt long-term planning and create uncertainty in financial markets. Controlling price hikes requires a balanced approach. Governments can adopt monetary policies to regulate the money supply and keep inflation in check. Fiscal policies that promote stability in public finances, investment in productive sectors, and support for vulnerable populations can also mitigate inflation. Additionally, maintaining a stable exchange rate and encouraging responsible pricing by businesses play a role. To stop or reduce price hikes, a multi-faceted strategy is needed. Governments must ensure transparency in pricing mechanisms and prevent monopolistic practices. Encouraging competition, investing in education and skill development, and diversifying the economy can enhance productivity and stabilize prices. Long-term economic planning and prudent fiscal management can create an environment that minimizes price hikes, fostering economic stability and improving the quality of life for citizens.

Explanation:
ক মূল্যস্ফীতি বা 'প্রাইস হাইক' হলো পণ্যের ও সেবার দাম সময়ের সঙ্গে সাধারণভাবে বাড়া; খ দাম বাড়ে কারণ উৎপাদন খরচ বেড়ে গেলে বিক্রেতারা দাম বাড়ায়, চাহিদা সরবরাহের চেয়ে বেশি হলে বা সরবরাহে বাধা পড়লে—এইগুলো সরবরাহ ও চাহিদার অনুপাত পরিবর্তিত করার ফলে ঘটে। গ মানুষ ক্ষতিগ্রস্ত হয় কারণ তাদের ক্রয়ক্ষমতা কমে যায়, নিত্যপ্রয়োজনীয় জিনিসের খরচ বেড়ে যায় এবং গরীব ও মধ্যবিত্ত সবচেয়ে বেশি প্রভাবিত হন। ঘ এটাকে নিয়ন্ত্রণে আনার জন্য সরকারের মুদ্রানীতি, ভর্তুকি, মজুদ-নিয়ন্ত্রণ ও স্থানীয় উৎপাদন বাড়ানো প্রয়োজন; ঙ আমাদেরও বাজেট মেনে চলা, অপচয় কমানো ও স্থানীয় ও মৌসুমী পণ্য কেনা উচিত—এসব প্রচেষ্টাই দাম স্থিতিশীল রাখতে সাহায্য করে।

Question:
Write a paragraph on 'An Ideal Student' based on the answers to the following questions:

(a) Who is an ideal student?

(b) What are the characteristics of an ideal student?

(c) What duties and responsibilities does and ideal student perform?

(d) What does he always think about?

(e) How is an ideal student treated by the general mass?

(f) Do you want to be an ideal student? Why?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
An Ideal Student

An ideal student is a beacon of dedication and excellence within an educational institution. Such a student embodies a set of exceptional qualities that inspire both peers and educators alike. They possess an insatiable curiosity and a genuine enthusiasm for learning, actively engaging in classroom discussions and seeking to expand their knowledge beyond the prescribed curriculum. An ideal student isn't merely focused on academic achievements; they also exhibit strong moral values, treating teachers, peers, and staff with respect and empathy. The characteristics of an ideal student are diverse and impactful. They display self-discipline, time management skills, and a strong work ethic. They approach challenges with perseverance and a growth mindset, viewing setbacks as opportunities for growth. An ideal student is open-minded, embracing diverse perspectives and ideas, fostering a harmonious learning environment. An ideal student shoulders responsibilities within and beyond the classroom. They actively participate in extracurricular activities, contribute to community service projects, and are often seen as role models by their peers. They diligently complete assignments, offer assistance to fellow students, and foster a collaborative learning atmosphere. An ideal student's thoughts are centered on personal growth and the pursuit of knowledge. They prioritize learning, constantly seeking ways to improve themselves academically and morally. They recognize that education is a lifelong journey and remain committed to continuous self-improvement. Within the general mass, an ideal student is admired and respected. Peers look up to them for guidance and inspiration, while teachers acknowledge their efforts and contributions. They are often seen as leaders and influencers, with their positive influence extending beyond the classroom. As an AI, I don't have personal aspirations, but aspiring to be an ideal student is a noble goal for anyone. Striving for excellence, both academically and morally, sets the foundation for personal success and contributes positively to the community. Being an ideal student not only opens doors to future opportunities but also shapes one's character and helps in building a strong foundation for a fulfilling life.

Explanation:
সমাধান: ক একজন আদর্শ ছাত্র হল এমন একজন যে শৃঙ্খলাবদ্ধ, পরিশ্রমী ও নৈতিকভাবে সৎ। খ তার বৈশিষ্ট্যের মধ্যে আছে নিয়ম মেনে চলা, সময়পালন, মনোযোগী পাঠাভ্যাস, নম্রতা ও সহযোগিতার মনোভাব। গ সে তার কর্তব্য—পাঠ প্রস্তুতি, শ্রেণীকক্ষের নিয়ম পালন, শিক্ষক ও সহপাঠীদের সহায়তা—দায়িত্বশীলভাবে করে এবং ঘ সবসময় পড়াশোনা, আত্মউন্নয়ন ও সমাজ-দেশের কল্যাণ ভাবেন। ঙ সাধারণ মানুষ তাকে শ্রদ্ধা ও ইতিবাচক দৃষ্টিতে দেখে, এবং চ আমি আদর্শ ছাত্র হতে চাই কারণ এতে ব্যক্তিগত উন্নতি ও সমাজের সেবা দুটোই সম্ভব।

ব্যাখ্যা: উপরের বর্ণনা সঠিক কারণ এতে আদর্শ ছাত্রের মূল গুণ, দায়িত্ব ও ভাবনা স্পষ্টভাবে বলা হয়েছে — যা একজন শিক্ষার্থীর আচরণ ও লক্ষ্য নির্ধারণ করে। সংক্ষিপ্ত ও সরল ভাষায় দেওয়ায় ছাত্ররা সহজে বোঝে কেন আদর্শ হওয়া জরুরি এবং কীভাবে তা অর্জন করা যায়।

Question #54 (ID: 209317)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph in about 200 words on "The Impact of Facebook on Teenagers".

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Impact of Facebook on Teenagers

The impact of Facebook on teenagers is a multifaceted phenomenon that has brought both positive and negative implications. On the positive side, Facebook has facilitated enhanced connectivity and communication among teenagers, allowing them to stay in touch with friends and family members regardless of geographical distance. It has provided a platform for self-expression, creativity, and sharing of personal experiences, helping adolescents build their social identities. Additionally, it can serve as a source of information and education, enabling them to engage in discussions on various subjects and current events. However, the influence of Facebook on teenagers is not devoid of challenges. Excessive usage can lead to negative mental health outcomes, as constant exposure to curated images and idealized lifestyles may breed feelings of inadequacy and low self-esteem. The quest for likes and validation can create a pressure to conform to certain norms and standards, potentially impacting their self-worth. The addictive nature of the platform can also disrupt real-world interactions, affect sleep patterns, and impede academic performance. Moreover, concerns about online privacy and exposure to inappropriate content raise flags regarding the safety of teenagers on Facebook. Cyberbullying and online harassment have become distressingly prevalent, causing emotional distress and psychological harm. The digital divide can exacerbate inequalities, as those without access to the platform might feel excluded from social circles. In response to these challenges, awareness campaigns, digital literacy education, and parental guidance play pivotal roles in helping teenagers navigate the world of Facebook responsibly. Encouraging a healthy balance between online and offline interactions, promoting critical thinking about the content they encounter, and fostering open communication about their online experiences can contribute to harnessing the positive potential of Facebook while minimizing its detrimental effects on teenagers' well-being.

Explanation:
Facebook has a mixed but powerful impact on teenagers’ lives. On the positive side, it helps teens stay connected with friends and family, discover communities with shared interests, and access news or educational resources quickly. These connections can support identity exploration and social belonging, especially for those who feel isolated offline. On the negative side, frequent Facebook use can encourage unhealthy social comparison, lower self-esteem, and increase exposure to cyberbullying and misinformation. Excessive screen time also distracts from homework, sleep, and face-to-face interactions, which can harm academic performance and mental wellbeing. Privacy risks are important too: teens may share personal information without understanding long-term consequences. The overall effect depends on how it is used—intentional, limited, and supervised use tends to produce benefits, while passive scrolling, constant comparison, and unmoderated interactions increase harm. Teaching digital literacy, setting sensible time limits, encouraging open communication about online experiences, and using privacy settings can help teens keep the advantages of Facebook while reducing its risks.

Question #55 (ID: 209318)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on 'The Victory Day' based on the answers to the following questions:

(a) When is our Victory Day? (b) Why is it called so? (c) What is the brief history behind it? (d) How do we observe the day? (e) What is the significance of the day?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Victory Day

Victory Day, celebrated on December 16th, marks a momentous occasion in the history of a nation and holds profound significance for its people. It commemorates the victory of a country's armed forces and citizens in a significant conflict, symbolizing their triumph over adversity and their unwavering spirit. In Bangladesh, Victory Day is celebrated to honor the triumph of the allied forces, comprised of Mukti Bahini (Liberation Army) and Indian military, against the Pakistani occupation forces in 1971, leading to the independence of Bangladesh from Pakistan. The brief history behind Victory Day centers on the Liberation War of 1971, a nine-month-long struggle that culminated in the creation of an independent nation. The Pakistani military's oppressive rule and atrocities prompted a spirited resistance, and the combined efforts of the local Mukti Bahini and the Indian armed forces eventually secured victory, resulting in the establishment of Bangladesh as a sovereign nation. On Victory Day, Bangladeshis engage in various activities to honor the sacrifices made by the freedom fighters. The day begins with a ceremonial raising of the national flag and the singing of the national anthem. Parades, processions, and cultural events are held across the country, involving citizens of all ages. Wreaths are laid at the National Martyrs' Memorial to pay homage to those who gave their lives for the nation's independence. The day is a time for reflection, remembrance, and gratitude for the freedom that was achieved through sacrifice and unity. The significance of Victory Day extends beyond its historical context; it serves as a reminder of the resilience and courage of a people determined to forge their destiny. It's a day of national pride and patriotism, inspiring the younger generation to cherish and safeguard the hard-won freedom while fostering a sense of unity among citizens. Victory Day stands as a testament to the power of collective action and the enduring human spirit in the face of adversity.

Explanation:
ক আমাদের বিজয় দিবস ১৬ ডিসেম্বর; এটি তাই বলা হয় কারণ খ ১৯৭১ সালের এই দিন পাকিস্তানি বাহিনী আনুষ্ঠানিকভাবে আত্মসমর্পণ করে ফলে বাংলাদেশ পূর্ণ মুক্তি লাভ করে। গ সংক্ষিপ্ত ইতিহাস—১৯৭১ সালের স্বাধীনতা সংগ্রাম ও লাখো শহীদের ত্যাগের পর মুক্তিযোদ্ধা ও মিত্র বাহিনীর জয় এই দিনটিকে নির্ধারণ করেছে। ঘ আমরা দিবসটি সরকারি ছুটি, শহীদদের প্রতি শ্রদ্ধা, মিছিল ও অনুষ্ঠান করে পালন করি এবং ঙ এর তাৎপর্য হলো স্বাধীনতা, জাতীয় একাত্মতা ও শহীদদের স্মরণ ধরে রাখা।

Question #56 (ID: 209319)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on the topic 'A Society I Dream of' in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions.

(a) What, according to your idea, is a good society?

(b) What are the aspects of a fair society?

(c) What may be your role to make that kind of society?

(d) How do you want to work to make it happen?

(e) What is the importance of making this sort of society?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Society I Dream of

The society I dream of is one characterized by harmony, equity, and empathy. In my vision, a good society is built upon the foundation of social justice, where every individual is valued and afforded equal opportunities regardless of their background. It prioritizes the well-being of its citizens, fostering an environment where basic needs such as education, healthcare, and housing are accessible to all. A fair society is marked by inclusivity, embracing diversity and celebrating the unique contributions of each member. To contribute to the realization of such a society, my role would involve active participation in advocacy, awareness campaigns, and community initiatives. I would strive to promote education and awareness about social issues, challenging stereotypes and biases that hinder progress. Collaborating with like-minded individuals and organizations, I would work to address systemic inequalities, support marginalized communities, and advocate for policies that uphold human rights and social welfare. My efforts to bring about this society would entail raising my voice against discrimination, engaging in volunteer work, and using various platforms to spread awareness and inspire positive change. By fostering empathy and encouraging dialogue, I aim to create spaces where individuals from diverse backgrounds can come together, learn from each other's experiences, and collectively contribute to a more just and compassionate society. The importance of creating such a society cannot be overstated. A fair and harmonious society not only enhances the quality of life for its citizens but also sets an example for future generations. It promotes a sense of belonging, strengthens social bonds, and ensures that everyone has the opportunity to thrive. By working towards this ideal society, we pave the way for a brighter future where justice, equality, and compassion prevail, creating a world that reflects the best of human values.

Explanation:
A society I dream of হবে এমন এক সমাজ যেখানে প্রতিটি মানুষ সম্মান, নিরাপত্তা এবং সুযোগ পায়। সেখানে বিচার ও আইন ন্যায়পরায়ণভাবে প্রয়োগিত হয়, আর প্রতিবন্ধকতা না দেখে দক্ষতার ওপর ভিত্তি করে সবাইকে শিক্ষা ও কর্মসংস্থান পাওয়া নিশ্চিত করা হয়। সামাজিক ও আর্থিক বৈষম্য কমাতে সুষ্ঠু নীতিমালা থাকবে এবং দুর্নীতির প্রবেশ নেই এমন প্রশাসন গড়তে হবে। নারী-पुरুষ, ধর্ম ও দলের ভেদাভেদ ভুলে সহযোগিতা ও সহানুভূতির পরিবেশ তৈরি হবে; পরিবেশ সুরক্ষা ও টেকসই উন্নয়নকে অগ্রাধিকার দেওয়া হবে। আমার ভূমিকা হবে আদর্শ আচরণ করা, গণতান্ত্রিক প্রক্রিয়ায় অংশগ্রহণ করা, দরিদ্র ও পিছিয়ে পড়াদের সাহায্য করা এবং শিক্ষা ও সচেতনতায় কাজ করা। আমি চাই স্থানীয় সংগঠন, স্বেচ্ছাসেবা ও শিক্ষা কার্যক্রমের মাধ্যমে বাস্তবে অংশগ্রহণ করব—জনসচেতনতা বাড়াব, সেবা প্রচেষ্টা চালাব এবং সঠিক নীতির পক্ষে ভোট ও সমর্থন দেব। এর ফলশ্রুতিতে সমাজে শান্তি, সাম্য ও আত্মসম্মানের উন্নতি হবে, অপরাধ ও দারিদ্র্য হ্রাস পাবে এবং ভবিষ্যৎ প্রজন্মের জন্য একটি স্থির ও সম্ভাবনাময় সমাজ গড়ে উঠবে।

ব্যাখ্যা: উপরের প্যারাগ্রাফটি প্রশ্নগুলোর সমন্বয়ে তৈরি—ভালো সমাজের বৈশিষ্ট্য, ন্যায়পরায়ণতার দিকসমূহ, ব্যক্তির ভূমিকা, বাস্তব কাজে কীভাবে অংশগ্রহণ করা যায় এবং এর গুরুত্ব সংক্ষেপে ব্যাখ্যা করা হয়েছে। এটি দেখায় যে সমাজ পরিবর্তন ব্যক্তিগত দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি ও সম্মিলিত প্রয়াস—দুইয়ের সমন্বয়ে সম্ভব।

Question:
Write a paragraph on "The Victory Day" in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions:

(a) When is our Victory Day?

(b) Why is it called so?

(c) What is the brief history behind it?

(d) How do we observe the day?

(e) What is the significance of the day?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Victory Day

Victory Day, celebrated on December 16th, holds a deeply cherished place in the hearts of Bangladeshis, commemorating a pivotal moment in their history. This day marks the triumphant culmination of the Liberation War in 1971 when the courageous citizens of Bangladesh, along with the valiant Mukti Bahini and the Indian armed forces, secured a hard-fought victory against the oppressive Pakistani occupation forces. The day is aptly named as it symbolizes the nation's resounding success in achieving independence and freedom from a suppressive regime. The history behind Victory Day is rooted in the nine-month-long struggle for autonomy and human rights. The Pakistani military's brutal rule and gross violations of human rights led to a determined resistance by the people of East Pakistan, now Bangladesh. The efforts of the Mukti Bahini and the Indian military eventually led to a historic victory, leading to the creation of an independent nation. The sacrifices made during this period, marked by immense human suffering, stand as a testament to the indomitable spirit of a people yearning for self-determination. The day is observed with solemnity and pride. The national flag is raised at dawn, and the country pays homage to the martyrs at the National Martyrs' Memorial. Parades, cultural events, and processions are held across the country, involving citizens from all walks of life. The day serves as a time of reflection, honoring the sacrifices made for freedom, and reinforcing a sense of national unity and identity. The significance of Victory Day transcends its historical context. It stands as a reminder of the nation's resilience, unity, and determination in the face of adversity. It fosters patriotism, instills a sense of gratitude towards the sacrifices of the past, and inspires present and future generations to safeguard the hard-won independence. Victory Day serves as a poignant symbol of the power of a united people striving for justice, dignity, and self-governance.

Explanation:
আমাদের বিজয় দিবস প্রতিবার ১৬ ডিসেম্বর পালন করা হয়। এটি বিজয় দিবস বলা হয় কারণ এই দিনে ১৯৭১ সালে পাকিস্তানি সেনাবাহিনী আনুষ্ঠানিকভাবে আত্মসমর্পণ করে এবং বাংলাদেশের স্বাধীনতা প্রতিষ্ঠার লড়াই সফল হয়ে যায়। সংক্ষিপ্ত ইতিহাস হিসেবে, ১৯৭১ সালের মুক্তিযুদ্ধে জাতি দীর্ঘপর্যায়ের দৃঢ় সংগ্রামের মধ্য দিয়ে গিয়েছিল; মার্চে স্বাধীনতার ঘোষণা ও চলমান রক্তক্ষয়ী সংঘর্ষের পরে ভারতীয় সহায়তায় মুক্তিযুদ্ধ চূড়ান্ত পর্যায়ে পৌঁছায় এবং ডিসেম্বরে বিজয় নিশ্চিত হয়। আমরা দিনটি বিভিন্নভাবে পালন করি—জাতীয় স্মৃতিসৌধে পুষ্পস্তবক অর্পণ, শহীদদের প্রতি শ্রদ্ধা, সামরিক প্যারেড, সরকারি ও সাংস্কৃতিক অনুষ্ঠান, স্কুল-কলেজে আলোচনা ও ইতিহাসচর্চা এবং গণমাধ্যমে স্মরণধর্মী প্রচার চালানো হয়। এ দিবসের তাৎপর্য হলো দেশের স্বাধীনতা ও মুক্তিযোদ্ধাদের অসীম ত্যাগ স্মরণ করা, জাতিগত ঐক্য ও জাতির গৌরব পুনর্মিলন করা। এই কারণে প্রতিটি প্রশ্নের উত্তর — তারিখ, নামকরণ, ইতিহাস, পালনপদ্ধতি ও তাৎপর্য— একসাথে মিলিয়ে দেখায় যে ১৬ ডিসেম্বর বাংলাদেশের স্বাধীনতার চূড়ান্ত বিজয়ের প্রতীক।

Question #58 (ID: 209321)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on 'Food Adulteration' in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions:10

(a) What do you mean by food adulteration? (b) How does food get adulterated? (c) Who are responsible for food adulteration? (d) What is the impact of adulterated food on our body? (e) What can be done to stop it?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Food adulteration

Food adulteration refers to the unethical practice of adding inferior, harmful, or substandard substances to food items in order to deceive consumers or enhance profits. This malicious practice jeopardizes public health and safety by compromising the quality and nutritional value of the food we consume. Adulteration can take various forms, such as adding synthetic colors, chemicals, preservatives, or using low-quality substitutes to increase quantity. The responsibility for food adulteration is shared among various stakeholders within the food supply chain. Unscrupulous producers, manufacturers, and suppliers driven by profit motives often engage in such practices to cut costs and maximize their gains. Retailers who fail to diligently scrutinize their suppliers and regulatory bodies that lack stringent enforcement also contribute to the issue. Consuming adulterated food has grave consequences for our health. Short-term effects can range from mild gastrointestinal discomfort to allergies and acute poisoning. Prolonged consumption of adulterated foods can lead to chronic health problems like organ damage, hormonal imbalances, and even cancer. Children, pregnant women, and the elderly are particularly vulnerable. To combat food adulteration, a multi-pronged approach is necessary. Strengthening food safety regulations and ensuring their strict enforcement is crucial. Regular monitoring, rigorous testing, and severe penalties for offenders can act as deterrents. Public awareness campaigns can educate consumers about identifying adulterated foods and encouraging them to report suspicious products. Additionally, supporting local and ethical food production practices can promote transparency and discourage shortcuts for profit. In conclusion, food adulteration is a serious concern that demands immediate attention and collective effort to ensure the availability of safe, nutritious, and authentic food for all. By holding those responsible accountable and fostering a culture of transparency, we can protect public health and integrity in the food industry.

Explanation:
খাবারে মান হ্রাস করে শারীরিক ক্ষতি সৃষ্টির উদ্দেশ্যে খাদ্যদ্রব্যে ভুল উপাদান, রং, রাসায়নিক বা সস্তা উপাদান মিশিয়ে রাখাকে খাবারের বদপ্রয়োগ বা Food Adulteration বলা হয়। সাধারণত তেল, দুধ, মশলা, মধু, এবং ফলের রস ইত্যাদি সস্তা কিংবা ক্ষতিকর পদার্থ দিয়ে পাতলা করে দেওয়া, রং যোগ করা, বা মেয়াদ বাড়ানোর জন্য কেমিক্যাল প্রয়োগের মাধ্যমে খাবার নষ্ট করা হয়। এ কাজের মূল কারণ লোকসানের ক্ষতি কমিয়ে বেশি মুনাফা অর্জন করার লোভ—যা উৎপাদক, পরিবেশক এবং খুচরা বিক্রেতা সকলের পক্ষ থেকেই ঘটতে পারে; দুর্বল আইন, শোকরাপত্রের অভাব ও ক্রেতাদের সচেতনতার অভাব এটিকে বাড়িয়ে তোলে। দূষিত খাবার খেলে ক্ষতিসাধ্য সংক্রমণ, পেটে ব্যথা, বমিভাব, দীর্ঘমেয়াদি রোগ যেমন কিডনী বা লিভারের ক্ষতিসহ ক্যান্সার ও পুষ্টিহীনতা দেখা দিতে পারে। প্রতিরোধের জন্য কঠোর আইন ও নজরদারি, নিয়মিত গুণ পরীক্ষণ, উৎপাদনে সঠিক মান বজায় রাখা, বিক্রেতা ও ক্রেতাদের প্রশিক্ষণ ও সচেতনতা বৃদ্ধির পাশাপাশি কড়া শাস্তি দরকার। ক্রেতাদেরই সতর্কতা—লেবেল দেখা, পারিতোষিক পরীক্ষক কেন্দ্রের সাহায্য নেয়া ও পরিচিত ব্রান্ড বেছে নেয়া—খাবারের বদপ্রয়োগ কমাতে সবচেয়ে দ্রুত ফলপ্রসূ ভূমিকা রাখতে পারে।

ক খাবারের বদপ্রয়োগ বলতে কী—কারণ: এটি খাবারের আসল গুণমান বদলে স্বাস্থ্যঝুঁকি তৈরি করে, তাই সংজ্ঞাটি সঠিক।  
খ কিভাবে হয়—কারণ: সস্তা উপাদান ও রং মেশানো বা রাসায়নিক প্রয়োগই প্রধান প্রক্রিয়া, তাই এগুলো মৌলিক কারণ।  
গ কে দায়ী—কারণ: উৎপাদক-পরিবেশক-বিক্রেতার লোভ ও দূরদর্শিতার অভাব মূল দায়িত্বশীল কারিগর।  
ঘ প্রভাব—কারণ: ক্ষতিকর উপাদান সরাসরি শরীরকে রোগগ্রস্ত করে, তাই সুস্পষ্ট স্বাস্থ্যঝুঁকি ওঠে।  
ঙ প্রতিরোধ—কারণ: আইন, পরীক্ষা ও সচেতনতা মিলে কারণটিকে রোধ করে; এগুলো কার্যকর হলে সমস্যা কমে।

Question #59 (ID: 209322)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “The Victory Day” in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions: (a) When is our Victory Day? (b) Why is it called so? (c) What is the brief history behind it? (d) How do we observe the day? (e) What is the significance of the day?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Victory Day

Victory Day, celebrated on December 16th, holds a special place in the heart of every Bangladeshi as it marks the glorious triumph of the nation in the Bangladesh Liberation War of 1971. This day commemorates the victory of the joint forces of the Mukti Bahini and the Indian Army over the Pakistani military, resulting in the liberation of Bangladesh from decades of oppression and struggle for independence. The history behind Victory Day is rooted in the nine-month-long Liberation War that began on March 26, 1971, following years of political and cultural suppression. The Pakistani military launched a brutal crackdown on the Bengali population, leading to widespread atrocities and loss of life. The war culminated on December 16th when the Pakistani forces surrendered, and Bangladesh emerged as an independent nation. The day is observed with great reverence and patriotism. The main events take place in the capital, Dhaka, where the National Memorial becomes the focal point of homage-paying. The national flag is hoisted at half-mast, and the day starts with a 31-gun salute. People from all walks of life participate in various ceremonies, parades, and cultural programs that pay tribute to the martyrs and honor the freedom fighters who sacrificed their lives for the nation's sovereignty. The significance of Victory Day goes beyond mere celebration; it serves as a reminder of the spirit of resilience, unity, and sacrifice that led to the birth of Bangladesh. It reinforces the values of freedom, democracy, and human rights that the nation upholds. This day also fosters a sense of national pride and instills in the younger generation an appreciation for the struggles and sacrifices made by their predecessors to secure their rights and identity. In conclusion, Victory Day is a momentous occasion that not only honors the valiant struggle for independence but also reinforces the ideals that shape the nation. It stands as a testament to the indomitable spirit of the Bangladeshi people and serves as a source of inspiration for generations to come.

Explanation:
Victory Day in Bangladesh is observed on 16 December each year to mark the decisive victory in the Liberation War of 1971, when Pakistani forces surrendered in Dhaka and Bangladesh secured its independence. It is called Victory Day because that date marks the end of nine months of struggle, widespread sacrifice, and the triumph of the Bengali people and their allies in establishing a sovereign nation. The brief history behind it includes the mass uprising beginning in March 1971, the formation of the Mukti Bahini (freedom fighters), severe repression and atrocities by occupying forces, and military intervention by India that helped bring about surrender on 16 December 1971. We observe the day with national ceremonies such as wreath-laying at the National Martyrs’ Memorial, official speeches, parades, cultural programs, flag hoisting, and moments of remembrance for those who died; schools and institutions hold events to teach younger generations about the struggle. The significance of the day lies in honoring the martyrs and freedom fighters, reaffirming national identity and unity, and reminding citizens of the values of sovereignty, justice, and the cost of freedom.

These answers are correct because they reflect the historical record: the military surrender occurred on 16 December 1971, which is why the date is commemorated as Victory Day. Observances and the day’s significance naturally follow from the fact that the event secured the nation’s independence and required large-scale sacrifice.

Question #60 (ID: 209323)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on ‘The Sundarbans’ on the basis of the answers to the following questions in about 200 words: (a) What type of forest is the Sundarbans? (b) What is the location of the Sundarbans? (c) Why is the Sundarbans famous? (d) What is the present condition of this forest? (e) What are the causes of destruction of the Sundarbans and what causes the extinction of tigers? (f) What role does the Sundarbans play in the national economy?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Sundarbans

The Sundarbans, renowned as the largest mangrove forest in the world, is a unique and vital ecosystem situated in the delta region of the Bay of Bengal. Stretching across the border between India and Bangladesh, this forest is characterized by its intricate network of waterways, tidal mudflats, and diverse plant and animal species. The Sundarbans holds global significance due to its rich biodiversity, featuring numerous rare and endangered species such as the Bengal tiger and the estuarine crocodile. Its fame is largely attributed to being the last bastion of the Bengal tiger, where these majestic creatures have adapted to a semi-aquatic life. However, the present condition of the Sundarbans is a cause for concern. The forest faces numerous threats, including rising sea levels, deforestation, pollution, and human encroachment. Climate change-induced sea-level rise poses a significant risk to this low-lying deltaic region, potentially leading to habitat loss and increased salinity of water bodies. Human activities like illegal logging, shrimp farming, and pollution from nearby industries further degrade this delicate ecosystem. These factors have led to a decline in the Bengal tiger population, pushing it closer to extinction. The destruction of the Sundarbans can be attributed to both natural and anthropogenic factors. Rising sea levels and erosion are natural challenges, while deforestation for agriculture and development exacerbate the situation. The extinction of tigers in the region is primarily driven by habitat loss, human-tiger conflicts, and poaching. Apart from its ecological significance, the Sundarbans also plays a crucial role in the national economy. It acts as a natural barrier, protecting coastal areas from storm surges and minimizing the impact of cyclones. The mangroves support various livelihoods through fishing, honey collection, and tourism. Furthermore, they contribute to carbon sequestration, helping mitigate the effects of climate change on a global scale. In conclusion, the Sundarbans' unique mangrove ecosystem faces a precarious future due to a combination of natural challenges and human activities. Efforts to preserve and restore this invaluable habitat are essential not only for safeguarding biodiversity but also for protecting coastal communities and sustaining local economies.

Question #61 (ID: 209324)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on ‘Pahela Baishakh’ in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions:

(i) What is the importance of Pahela Baishakh to the people of Bangladesh? (ii) What do people do on Pahela Baishakh? (iii) What is the most impressive part of the celebration? (iv) How does the festival uphold our culture? (V) What benefits do we reap from this kind of festivals?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Pahela Baishakh

Pahela Baishakh, the Bengali New Year, holds immense importance to the people of Bangladesh as it marks the beginning of a new agricultural cycle and carries cultural significance that resonates deeply within the nation. On this day, people celebrate with great enthusiasm, embracing their heritage and traditions. They wear colorful traditional attire, often in shades of red and white, and participate in various cultural events, fairs, and processions that take place across the country. The celebrations on Pahela Baishakh involve traditional music, dance, and art, reflecting the rich cultural heritage of Bangladesh. The most impressive part of the celebration is the Mangal Shobhajatra procession, a vibrant and colorful parade that symbolizes the people's resistance against oppression and their commitment to a diverse and inclusive society. Pahela Baishakh is not just a festivity but a cultural manifestation that upholds the essence of Bengali identity. It brings people together irrespective of their background, fostering unity and harmony. The festival showcases traditional foods, crafts, and performances, preserving and promoting the unique cultural heritage of the country. Such festivals contribute significantly to our cultural preservation and tourism sectors. They attract both domestic and international visitors, boosting local economies and providing opportunities for artisans and performers to showcase their talents. Moreover, these celebrations strengthen the sense of community, identity, and belonging among the people, reaffirming their roots and encouraging them to take pride in their heritage. In conclusion, Pahela Baishakh is more than just a New Year celebration; it's a vital cultural event that connects people to their history, traditions, and values. By coming together in the spirit of unity and celebration, individuals not only honor their past but also contribute to the prosperity of their future.

Explanation:
পহেলা বৈশাখ হলো বাংলাদেশের সাংস্কৃতিক ও সামাজিক নববর্ষের উদযাপন, যা ধর্ম-বর্ণ নির্বিশেষে মানুষের মধ্যে ঐক্য, আশা ও জাতীয় পরিচয় জাগায়; কারণ এটি লোকসংস্কৃতি, ভোগচার্য্য ও ঐতিহ্যকে একত্র করে। মানুষ মঙ্গল শোভাযাত্রা, নাচ-গান, তাজা পোশাক পরা, পান্তা-ইলিশসহ ঐতিহ্যবাহী খাবারভোগ, মেলা ও ব্যবসায়িক নতুন হিসাব খোলার মাধ্যমে দিনটি উদযাপন করে; সবচেয়ে নতি: মঙ্গল শোভাযাত্রার রঙীন মুখোশ এবং অনুষ্ঠানিক শোভা যা ইউনেস্কো স্বীকৃত—এটিই সবচেয়ে প্রভাবশালী অংশ। এই উৎসব আমাদের লোকশিল্প, ভাষা ও রীতিনীতি সংরক্ষণ করে, সম্প্রদায়িক বন্ধন শক্তিশালী করে এবং পর্যটন ও ক্ষুদ্র-ব্যবসাকে ত্বরান্বিত করে—এসব কারণেই পহেলা বৈশাখ আমাদের সংস্কৃতি ও অর্থনীতির জন্য গুরুত্বপূর্ণ।

Question #62 (ID: 209325)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on Climate Change’ in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions:

(a) What is climate change? (b) What are the causes of climate change? (0) What are the impacts of climate change? (d) How is climate change a threat to Bangladesh? (e) How can climate change be minimized?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Climate change

Climate change refers to the long-term alteration of Earth's average weather patterns, encompassing shifts in temperature, precipitation, and various climatic factors. This phenomenon is primarily driven by human activities that release significant amounts of greenhouse gases into the atmosphere, such as carbon dioxide from burning fossil fuels, deforestation, and industrial processes. These gases trap heat, leading to a warming of the planet known as the greenhouse effect. The consequences of climate change are far-reaching and include more frequent and intense heatwaves, extreme weather events, rising sea levels, melting glaciers, and disruptions in ecosystems. In Bangladesh, a country situated in a low-lying delta region, climate change poses severe threats. The nation is vulnerable to rising sea levels, which can lead to coastal erosion, inundation of lands, and displacement of millions of people. Additionally, erratic monsoon patterns can cause devastating floods and prolonged droughts, impacting agriculture and food security. The increased frequency of cyclones also endangers lives and livelihoods, particularly in densely populated coastal areas. To mitigate climate change, international cooperation is crucial. Reduction of greenhouse gas emissions through transitioning to renewable energy sources, enhancing energy efficiency, afforestation, and sustainable land management can play a pivotal role. Moreover, adopting climate-resilient practices, building robust infrastructure, and implementing early warning systems can help countries like Bangladesh adapt to the changing climate. Public awareness campaigns, education, and policy reforms are essential to foster a collective commitment to addressing this global challenge and safeguarding the planet for future generations.

Explanation:
Climate change is the long-term alteration of average weather patterns, primarily global warming driven by increased concentrations of greenhouse gases that trap heat in the atmosphere; this explanation is correct because physics (the greenhouse effect) shows how gases like carbon dioxide and methane increase radiative forcing and raise temperatures. Major causes include burning fossil fuels, deforestation, intensive agriculture, and some industrial processes that release carbon dioxide, methane and nitrous oxide; these human activities elevate greenhouse gas levels beyond natural variability, which explains why recent warming is linked to us. The impacts are higher temperatures, more frequent and intense heatwaves, changing rainfall patterns, stronger storms, melting glaciers and rising sea levels, all of which harm ecosystems, food production, water supplies and human health. Bangladesh is especially threatened because it is a low-lying delta: sea-level rise, coastal erosion, saline intrusion, increased flooding and stronger cyclones directly damage homes, crops and infrastructure, forcing displacement and economic loss. To minimize climate change we must reduce emissions through energy efficiency, renewables, stopping deforestation and shifting to sustainable agriculture, while strengthening adaptation—early warning systems, resilient infrastructure, mangrove restoration and international climate finance. Together mitigation and adaptation address both the root causes and the local threats, which is why these responses are the correct and effective approach.

Question #63 (ID: 209326)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on ‘Diaspora’ on the basis of the answers to the following questions in about 200 words

(a) What is diaspora? (b) What are the major causes of diaspora? (c) Who were the greatest displaced people in the history? (d) Do you find any diaspora in recent times? (e) What are the consequences of diaspora?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Diaspora

Diaspora refers to the dispersion or migration of a group of people from their original homeland to other parts of the world. This movement often occurs due to various factors such as conflict, economic opportunities, political instability, or the search for better living conditions. One of the major historical instances of diaspora was the Jewish dispersion, known as the Jewish Diaspora, which occurred as a result of conquests, conflicts, and exile. In recent times, various diasporas have emerged due to globalization, urbanization, and the pursuit of education and employment opportunities in foreign countries. The consequences of diaspora are multifaceted. On one hand, it can result in cultural enrichment as diaspora communities often retain and celebrate their cultural heritage, sharing it with their host countries. This cultural diversity can lead to a vibrant and pluralistic society. However, diaspora can also lead to challenges such as identity struggles, loss of connections to the homeland, and feelings of displacement. Additionally, diaspora communities might face discrimination or struggle to integrate fully into the new societies they inhabit. Yet, diaspora communities can also wield economic, social, and political influence both in their host countries and back in their homelands, through remittances, advocacy, and the establishment of transnational networks. In conclusion, diaspora is a complex phenomenon that involves the dispersal of people from their homeland for various reasons. It has shaped history and continues to be a relevant aspect of contemporary society, impacting both the individuals and the countries involved. While it brings about cultural diversity and potential benefits, it also presents challenges that must be navigated by those who experience it.

Explanation:
ক দায়াস্পোরা হলো কোনো দেশের বা জাতির মানুষের বৃহৎ পরিমাণে দেশবর্হিভব বা ছড়িয়ে পড়া, যার ফলেই তারা নিজেদের মূলভূমির সঙ্গে সাংস্কৃতিক, সামাজিক বা অর্থনৈতিকভাবে সম্পর্ক রেখে চলে; এটি সাধারণত স্বেচ্ছাগত বা জোরপূর্বক উভয় কারণে ঘটে। খ প্রধান কারণগুলোর মধ্যে যুদ্ধ ও রাজনৈতিক নিপীড়ন, ধর্মীয় বা জাতিগত উৎপীড়ন, অর্থনৈতিক সুযোগের অনুপস্থিতি, প্রাকৃতিক দুর্যোগ ও পরিবেশগত পরিবর্তন এবং ঔপনিবেশিক বা শ্রমবাজারভিত্তিক বাস্তবতা রয়েছে। গ ইতিহাসে বড় মাত্রার বিচ্ছিন্নতার উদাহরণগুলো হল ইহুদিদের দীর্ঘকালীন দায়াস্পোরা, আফ্রিকানদের ট্রান্স-আটলান্টিক দাসত্ব থেকে সৃষ্টি হওয়া আফ্রিকান দায়াস্পোরা, এবং ১৯৪৭ সালের ভারত-পাকিস্তান বিভাগের সময়ের একক বৃহৎ উদ্ভট বাস্তুচ্যুতি। ঘ সাম্প্রতিক সময়ে সিরীয় ও আফগান শরণার্থী সমস্যা, রোহিঙ্গাদের নির্বাসন, ভেনেজুয়েলা ও ইউক্রেন থেকে প্রবাসীদের বর্ধিত প্রবাহ স্পষ্ট দায়াস্পোরা হিসেবে দেখা যায়। ঙ দায়াস্পোরা সামাজিক ও অর্থনৈতিক উভয় ধরনের প্রভাব ফেলে—অন্যদিকে প্রবাসীরা মূলভূমিকে রেমিট্যান্স, জ্ঞান ও সাংস্কৃতিক বিনিময় দেয়; অন্যদিকে হোস্ট দেশে চাপ, পরিচয় সংকট, এবং উৎসভূমিতে মেধা-নিষ্ক্রমণ ও জনসংখ্যাগত পরিবর্তন ঘটতে পারে। এসব উদাহরণ ও কারণ দেখায় কেন এসব মানুষগুলোকে “দায়াস্পোরা” বলা হয়: তারা প্রায়ই বাধ্যতামূলকভাবে বা স্থায়ীভাবে স্থান বদলে মূলভূমির সঙ্গে সম্পর্ক বজায় রাখে।

Question #64 (ID: 209327)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “Digital Bangladesh” on the basis of the answers to the following questions in about 200 words: (a) What is Digital Bangladesh? (b) How can we achieve it? (c) What steps should be taken by the government to execute it? (d) How can students take part in it? (e) Is the idea too ambitious?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Digital Bangladesh

"Digital Bangladesh" is a vision and goal that aims to transform Bangladesh into a technologically advanced and digitally empowered nation. The concept envisions utilizing digital technology to enhance governance, education, healthcare, and various sectors, ultimately leading to socioeconomic development and improved quality of life for its citizens. Achieving a Digital Bangladesh involves leveraging information and communication technology (ICT) to connect rural and urban areas, bridge the digital divide, and promote e-governance and digital literacy. To realize this vision, concerted efforts from all sectors are required. The government plays a pivotal role in executing this plan by investing in ICT infrastructure, promoting digital education, fostering e-governance, and encouraging innovation and entrepreneurship in the technology sector. Initiatives like e-governance platforms, digital payment systems, and digital citizen services contribute to the transformation process. Students can play a significant role in the journey towards a Digital Bangladesh. By embracing digital education, gaining proficiency in ICT skills, and participating in digital literacy programs, students can contribute to the dissemination of technological knowledge within their communities. They can also engage in technology-driven projects that address local challenges, contributing to sustainable development. While the vision of a Digital Bangladesh is ambitious, it is not unattainable. The rapid advancement of technology and the increasing integration of digital solutions into various aspects of life indicate that the idea is both realistic and necessary for national development. However, challenges such as infrastructural gaps, access disparities, and cybersecurity concerns must be addressed for the vision to be fully realized. In conclusion, Digital Bangladesh signifies the transformation of the nation through digital technology, enhancing various sectors and improving citizens' lives. By leveraging the potential of ICT, embracing digital education, and fostering innovation, Bangladesh can achieve its goal of becoming a digitally empowered nation, though it will require collaborative efforts from the government, citizens, and various stakeholders to ensure its success.

Explanation:
Digital Bangladesh is a national vision to transform Bangladesh into a knowledge-based, technology-driven society by using information and communication technology (ICT) to improve governance, education, health, and the economy. To achieve it we need widespread internet connectivity, reliable power, affordable devices, strong digital infrastructure (data centers, cloud services), interoperable e-government platforms, digital literacy for all, and encouragement of innovation and IT entrepreneurship. The government should invest in broadband networks, expand rural connectivity, modernize schools and hospitals with ICT, enact clear cyber-law and data-protection frameworks, strengthen cybersecurity, provide incentives for tech startups, and train teachers and civil servants to deliver digital services. Students can take part by learning basic and advanced ICT skills, using e-learning resources, joining coding clubs and hackathons, creating useful digital content and apps, and promoting responsible online behavior. The idea is ambitious but realistic: with phased planning, sustained public and private investment, inclusive policies, and active participation from citizens—especially youth—Digital Bangladesh can be realized and will raise productivity, transparency, and access to services across the country.

This paragraph is correct because it links the definition of Digital Bangladesh to concrete means (infrastructure, policy, skills) and roles (government, students). Understanding is aided by showing practical steps and emphasizing that ambition becomes achievable through phased actions and broad participation.

Question #65 (ID: 209328)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on Folk Music’ by answering the following questions in about 200 words:

(a) What is folk music? (b) What are the components of folk music? (e) Why is folk music not sophisticated (d) Who are the contributors of folk music in Bangladesh? (e) What kind of role does folk music play in our social and cultural life?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Folk Music

Folk music is a genre that encompasses the traditional melodies, rhythms, and lyrical narratives of a particular community or culture. It is an artistic expression of the people, often passed down orally from one generation to another, reflecting the history, values, and experiences of a society. The components of folk music include simple melodies, straightforward lyrics, and often the use of traditional instruments. Its simplicity is a result of its organic growth over time, evolving naturally within communities rather than through formal composition. This lack of sophistication, however, should not be mistaken for insignificance, as folk music carries deep emotional resonance and authenticity. In Bangladesh, folk music finds its roots in the diverse ethnic groups that make up the country. Contributors to Bangladeshi folk music include Bauls, mystic troubadours who sing about spiritual love and unity; Bhatiali musicians, who celebrate the lives of fishermen through their songs; and the Baul-Fakir tradition, which fuses mystical elements with musical expression. These musicians contribute to a rich tapestry of musical traditions that are woven into the fabric of the nation. Folk music holds a pivotal role in the social and cultural life of communities. It serves as a repository of cultural heritage, preserving historical narratives, local customs, and collective memories. Through folk music, communities strengthen their bonds, passing on shared experiences and wisdom. Moreover, folk music often addresses social issues, conveying messages of unity, resistance, and hope. In celebrations and rituals, folk music sets the rhythm of life, fostering a sense of identity and belonging. In essence, folk music is the soulful heartbeat of cultural continuity, bridging generations and fostering a sense of belonging and pride.

Explanation:
ক ফোক সঙ্গীত হলো কোনো নির্দিষ্ট শ্রেণির শিল্পী নয়, বরং গ্রামের সাধারণ মানুষদের মৌখিকভাবে প্রজন্ম থেকে প্রজন্মে স্থানান্তরিত গান ও বাদ্যযন্ত্র; এটি লোকজ জীবনের অনুভূতি, কাজ, গল্প ও আচার-অনুষ্ঠান বহন করে — তাই এটিকে ফোক বলা হয়। খ উপাদানগুলো হলো সরল লিরিক (কথা), স্থানীয় ছন্দ ও মাত্রা, ব্যবহারিক বাদ্যযন্ত্র (যেমন ঢাক, খোল, ইসক-out), এবং গায়কীর আদিবাসী বা ধর্মীয় রীতিনীতি; এগুলো মিলে গানটির গঠন ও অর্থ গড়ে তোলে। গ ফোক সঙ্গীতকে সাধারণত 'সরল' বা 'অলংকারহীন' মনে করা হয় কারণ এটি গুরুতর সঙ্গীতশিল্পীর মতো জটিল সুরসূত্র নয়, বরং দৈনন্দিন জীবনের সরল আবেগ ও প্রয়োজন মেটাতে তৈরি — মৌখিক রীতি ও পুনরাবৃত্তি এতে বেশি। ঘ contributors বা প্রধান ধারকরা হলেন গ্রামের গায়ক, বাউল, ফেরিওয়ালা, নৌকো গায়ক (ভাটিয়ালি) এবং সমাজের সাধারণ লোকেরা যারা উৎসব, বিবাহ, কাজের সময় ও ধর্মীয় অনুষ্ঠানে গান পরিবেশন করে। ঙ সামাজিক ও সাংস্কৃতিক জীবনে ফোক সঙ্গীতের ভূমিকা বিশাল: এটি ইতিহাস ও নৈতিকতা সংরক্ষণ করে, সামাজিক ঐক্য গড়ে তোলে, উৎসব ও কাজকে ritmo দেয় এবং সাধারণ মানুষের অনুভূতি ও পরিচয় প্রকাশের প্রধান মাধ্যম।

Question #66 (ID: 209329)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Dhaka Board, Dinajpur Board, Sylhet Board | Tags: Dhaka Board, Dinajpur Board, Sylhet Board, Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “Food Adulteration” on the basis of the answers to the following questions in about 200 words.

(a) What is food adulteration? (b) How is food adulterated? (c) Who are responsible for food adulteration? (d) What is the impact of adulterated food on our body? (e) What can be done to stop it? 8. The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Food Adulteration

Food adulteration refers to the unethical practice of adding inferior, harmful, or substandard substances to food items in order to increase quantity, enhance appearance, or deceive consumers about the quality of the product. This malicious act compromises the safety and health of consumers, leading to a range of detrimental consequences. Food can be adulterated through various means, including adding artificial colors, synthetic flavors, and chemical preservatives. Common examples involve mixing water with milk, adding chalk powder to spices, or using lower quality oils. The responsibility for food adulteration lies with unscrupulous manufacturers, suppliers, and middlemen who prioritize profit over public health. Adulterated food can have severe impacts on human health. Consumption of adulterated food can lead to short-term effects such as nausea, vomiting, diarrhea, and stomach cramps. In the long run, regular intake of adulterated food can result in chronic health issues like gastrointestinal disorders, organ damage, and even life-threatening diseases. Children, pregnant women, and the elderly are particularly vulnerable to these health risks. To counter food adulteration, a multi-pronged approach is essential. Strengthening regulatory bodies and enforcing stringent laws can act as a deterrent to those involved in adulteration. Regular inspections, quality checks, and strict penalties for offenders can help maintain the integrity of the food supply chain. Public awareness campaigns are crucial to educating consumers about the dangers of consuming adulterated food and encouraging them to report any suspicious products. Additionally, promoting the use of food testing kits and technologies can empower consumers to check the quality of products at their end. In conclusion, food adulteration is a grave issue that threatens public health and safety. Unethical practices by individuals and businesses harm consumers and erode trust in the food industry. Efforts from regulatory authorities, manufacturers, and consumers are imperative to eradicate this menace. By fostering a culture of transparency, accountability, and ethical responsibility, we can ensure that the food we consume is safe, nutritious, and free from adulterants.

Explanation:
খাদ্য ভেজালকরণ হল খাদ্যের মধ্যে নিম্নমানের উপাদান, রং, রাসায়নিক বা পানি মিশিয়ে তার গুণমান, পুষ্টিমান ও নিরাপত্তা খর্ব করা। ভেজাল সাধারণত ঘটে নিম্নমানের বা সস্তা দ্রব্য মিশিয়ে, দুধে পানি বা মোটানো, মশলায় দারুণ জাগোপোনা উপাদান বা সল্ট-পেপারের বদলে রঙীন কণিকা দেওয়া, তেল পুনরায় ব্যবহার করা, এবং ফল-শাক-পাচকাদিতে কৃত্রিম রং বা কনজার্ভেটিভ যোগ করে। দায়ী লোকেরা প্রায়শই আর্থিক লাভের জন্য কৃতকম কৃত্য করে — অনৈতিক ব্যবসায়ী, খাদ্যকারখানা, মাঝামাঝি ব্যবসায়ী এবং কখনও কখনও অনিয়ন্ত্রিত বিক্রেতারা। ভেজাল খাবার শরীরে তীব্র ও দীর্ঘমেয়াদী ক্ষতি করতে পারে: পেটব্যথা, অপেন বা বিষক্রিয়া, পুষ্টিহীনতা, যৌন ও প্রজনন সমস্যা, কিডনি-যকृत ক্ষতি, এবং কিছু ক্ষেত্রে ক্যান্সার সহ দীর্ঘস্থায়ী রোগের ঝুঁকি বাড়ে। এ রোধে দরকার কড়া আইন ও নিয়ন্ত্রক মনিটরিং, নিয়মিত পরীক্ষণ ও সার্টিফিকেশন, কড়া জরিমানা ও শাস্তি, ভোক্তা সচেতনতা ও শিক্ষণ, এবং নিরাপদ সরবরাহ শৃঙ্খলা গড়ে তোলা—যেমন লেবেল যাচাই, ব্র্যান্ড-ভিত্তিক কেনাকাটা ও সরকারি পরীক্ষাগারে নমুনা পাঠানো। এই সকল উদ্যোগ মিলে খাদ্য ভেজাল কমিয়ে জনস্বাস্থ্য রক্ষা করা সম্ভব।

Question #67 (ID: 209330)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Chittagong Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board | Tags: Chattogram Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board, Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a paragraph on “The Historic Speech of 7th March” in about 200 words based on the answers to the following questions.

(i) When was the speech delivered?

(ii) Where was the speech delivered?

(iii) Who were addressed in this speech?

(iv) How was the speech related to our national history?

(v) How is the speech evaluated internationally?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Historic Speech of 7th March

The historic speech of 7th March stands as a cornerstone of our nation's narrative, delivered on a significant date in 1971. On this momentous occasion, the speech was given by Sheikh Mujibur Rahman, addressing a massive gathering at the Race Course Ground (now Suhrawardy Udyan) in Dhaka, Bangladesh. The audience that gathered with bated breath included thousands of fervent Bengalis who yearned for autonomy and a rightful place within their own country. This seminal speech was an unequivocal call for unity, self-determination, and a demand for justice, echoing the collective sentiment of a nation under oppression. In the annals of our national history, the speech is hailed as a galvanizing force that ignited the flames of resistance against subjugation and injustice. It effectively marked the clarion call for the Liberation War of 1971, which ultimately led to the birth of an independent Bangladesh. The speech's resonant words continue to inspire generations, encapsulating the fervor for freedom and the indomitable spirit of a people. Internationally, the speech is evaluated with reverence and awe, recognized as a masterpiece of oratory that catalyzed a crucial turning point in global history. It is celebrated for its power to unite and mobilize, transcending borders and language barriers to strike a chord with oppressed populations across the world. The speech of 7th March is a testament to the enduring strength of words and their ability to shape destinies, evoking a spirit of resilience that continues to reverberate throughout the world.

Explanation:
৭ই মার্চ ১৯৭১ তারিখে ঢাকা রমনা রেসকোর্স (বর্তমানে সোহরাওয়ার্দী উদ্যান) এ অনুষ্ঠিত জনসভায় জাতির পিতা শেখ মুজিবুর রহমান যে ভাষণ দিলেন তা বাংলাদেশের স্বাধীনতা আন্দোলনের এক মাইলফলক। বিশাল জনসমক্ষে তিনি পাকিস্তানি শাসকবৃন্দের উপদেশ ও হত্যার আগ্রাসন বর্বরতা মোকাবিলায় জনগণকে ঐক্যবদ্ধ হয়ে প্রস্তুত থাকার আহ্বান জানান; বক্তৃতাটিতে স্বাধীনতার প্রতিশ্রুতি সরাসরি বলা না হলেও তা কার্যত স্বাধীনতার ঘোষণা ও সশস্ত্র সংগ্রামের পথে জাতিকে অনুপ্রাণিত করে। ভাষণটি ছিল সশস্ত্র মুক্তিযুদ্ধের নৈতিক ও রাজনৈতিক ভিত্তি গঠনের অনন্য উৎস, কারণ এতে মানুষের মনোবল বাড়ে এবং রাজশাহীর প্রতি অসহযোগিতা ও বিক্ষোভের আদেশ-প্রেরণা মজবুত হয়। আন্তর্জাতিকভাবে এই ভাষণকে মহান রাজনৈতিক বক্তৃতা হিসেবে স্বীকৃতি দেয়া হয়েছে; ২০১৭ সালে UNESCO-এর মেমোরি অব দ্য ওয়ার্ল্ড রেজিস্ট্রিতে ৭ই মার্চের ভাষণ অন্তর্ভুক্ত করা হয় যার মাধ্যমে এটি বিশ্বের ঐতিহাসিক নথির মর্যাদা পায় এবং উপনিবেশবাদ-অধিকার সংগ্রামের প্রতীকে পরিণত হয়।

ব্যাখ্যা: উপরের তথ্যগুলো ঐতিহাসিক দলিল, সাক্ষী ও আন্তর্জাতিক সংস্থার স্বীকৃতির উপর ভিত্তি করে সুনির্দিষ্টভাবে প্রতিষ্ঠিত—৭ই মার্চের তারিখ, স্থান ও বক্তৃতার প্রভাব নথিভুক্ত; UNESCO স্বীকৃতি আন্তর্জাতিক মূল্যায়ন হিসেবে ভাষণের গুরুত্ব প্রমাণ করে।

Question #69 (ID: 209206)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board, Barisal Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, you are Mahin. Your friend Abir is very afraid of English. Now, write a letter to him describing how to be competent in English.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

12 Mirpur Road

Shahabag, Dhaka

23 January 2023

Dear Abit,

I received your letter yesterday. In your letter, you talked about your weakness in English. You have also asked me

for some suggestions on how to be competent in English. Here I go with my suggestion. In order to be competent in English, you have to acquire all the four skills of English, which are reading, writing,

listening and speaking. At first, you should attend your English classes regularly and listen to your teachers attentively. You should also watch English programmes on TV and listen to the English programmes on radio. All these will improve your listening skill. Secondly, you should speak in English with your English teacher, and interact with family members and friends for daily activities in English too. Self-talk in English also helps a lot in developing speaking skills. Thirdly, to improve your reading skill, you should often read and try to understand story books, illustrated books, daily or weekly English newspapers, etc. While reading, if you fail to understand the meanings of some new words, you should try to guess their meanings from the context. If you can't, you should look them up in a good dictionary. You should also practice 'Reading Comprehensions', cloze passages, etc. Besides, you have to study grammar for developing writing skills. Then, you should regularly write paragraphs, compositions, etc. off-hand and get them checked by your English teachers. Furthermore, you can keep a diary and write a few pages every day. These things will improve your writing skill. By doing the above activities, you can be competent in English. I hope to hear from you soon. Convey my best regards to your parents. Take care.

Yours ever,

Mahin

Explanation:
লেখাটি সঠিক কারণ এতে ভীতির প্রতি সহমর্মিতা দেখানো হয়েছে এবং একাধিক ব্যবহারযোগ্য ধাপ—নিয়মিত অনুশীলন, পড়া-শোনা, বাক্যভাণ্ডার ও ব্যাকরণ শেখা—দিয়ে নির্দিষ্ট লক্ষ্য দেখানো হয়েছে। মূল ধারণা হলো ভাষা দক্ষতা একরাতে হয় না; ধারাবাহিকতা, বাস্তব ব্যবহার (বক্তৃতা ও শ্রবণ) ও ভ্রমণ/মাধ্যমের মাধ্যমে অভ্যাস করলে উন্নতি হয়। বন্ধুবৎসল স্বর ও ছোট ছোট বাস্তব উপদেশ ভয়ের মনোভাব কমায় এবং অনুপ্রেরণা জোগায়, তাই এমন একটা চিঠি কার্যকর।

Medical Hostel

Mymensingh

Dear Atif,

How are you? I came to know from Maa that you do not read English newspapers at all. Well, there are a lot of benefits of reading English newspapers. Let me tell you about its benefits.

By reading English newspapers, you will get to know the news of our country and other countries of the world. In this way, you will remain updated. More importantly, reading English newspapers will enhance your knowledge in English. You may come across many new vocabularies that you are not acquainted with. In that case, you can infer the meaning from the context and then, look up the dictionary for help. Nowadays, English newspapers are available on internet. You can find a number of English newspapers on net for free. Besides, you will find English newspapers on your college common room. You can also ask the hawker to deliver more English newspapers at home.

Wish you a bright future. How are Etu and Ruma? Convey my regards to Baba and Maa.

Yours ever.

Alif

To be effective, the letter should be encouraging and offer simple, actionable tips (choose easy papers, read daily, note new words).

Question:
Write a letter to your younger brother/sister advising him/her not to share fake or baseless news on his/her social media account.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
House: 12/3, Zakir Hussain Road,

Mohammadpur, Dhaka-1207

24 August 2023

Dear Ameerah,

I hope this letter finds you in good health. I know you miss me a lot, because I have been missing you too. Thanks to Facebook; however, sometimes I feel that you are right here beside me. Everything you keep sharing makes me feel that we are enjoying all together!

On that note, I would like to tell you to be very careful about sharing fake or baseless news on your social media accounts. We've both watched cases where people have been misguided into believing these news stories. Imagine the kind of pain one would feel if the news was on a particularly sensitive topic, or regarding something that was very close to their heart. Wouldn't you feel guilty for causing somebody immeasurable pain from seemingly just a simple share? As your elder sister and your biggest well-wisher, I would suggest that you try to be more careful and only share authentic news articles that have been verified from multiple sources, It would also be wise to verify the news because you could easily be incriminated under the Digital Security Acter the ICT Act of Bangladesh, which would have a lasting impact on your life and career. I hope you understand that I am coming from a place of love and concern,

Take care, my sweet little sister. Hope to see you soon.

Lots of love,

Anika

Explanation:

Question #78 (ID: 209151)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, you are Ratul. Write an e-mail to your younger brother narrating the benefits of reading newspapers daily.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To :

Subject: The Wonderful World of Newspapers: Why Reading Daily Matters

Hey [Younger Brother's Name],

I hope you're doing well and enjoying your time. I wanted to share something with you that I think will be really beneficial for your overall growth – the habit of reading newspapers daily.

I know it might not sound super exciting at first, but trust me, reading newspapers can open up a whole new world of knowledge and awareness. Here are some great reasons why you should consider making this a part of your daily routine:

Stay Informed: Newspapers are a treasure trove of current events, both local and global. By reading them regularly, you'll be up to date with what's happening in the world around you. It's an excellent way to be informed about current affairs, politics, science, technology, and more.

Improve Language Skills: Reading newspapers exposes you to a wide range of vocabulary and writing styles. This will enhance your language skills, making you a better communicator in both spoken and written forms.

Critical Thinking: Many articles present different perspectives on the same issue. Reading diverse viewpoints can help you develop critical thinking skills, as you learn to analyze and form your own opinions.

Expand Knowledge: Newspapers cover a variety of topics, from science and history to sports and entertainment. This helps you explore new subjects and learn about things you might not have encountered otherwise.

Develop Reading Habit: Cultivating the habit of reading newspapers daily can foster a love for reading in general. This can lead to a lifelong habit of seeking knowledge and exploring the written word.

Build Awareness: Newspapers often cover social issues, health tips, and practical advice. By reading them, you'll gain valuable insights that can help you make informed decisions in various aspects of your life.

Discussion and Debate: The topics you read about in newspapers can become great conversation starters with family and friends. You'll be surprised how engaging and insightful discussions can arise from these topics.

Remember, it's not about reading the entire newspaper cover to cover. Start with a few articles that catch your interest and gradually build your reading stamina. Over time, you'll find it both enjoyable and beneficial.

So, give it a try, little bro! Make reading newspapers a part of your daily routine, and you'll be amazed at the positive impact it can have on your life.

Take care and keep shining!

Warm regards,

Ratul

Explanation:
এই ই‑মেইলটি সঠিক কারণ ভাইকে ব্যক্তিগত ও বন্ধুসুলভ ভাষায় দৈনন্দিন সংবাদপত্র পড়ার লাভগুলো সহজ উদাহরণ ও অনুপ্রেরণার মাধ্যমে বোঝায়। একটি ভালো ই‑মেইলে সাধারণত সম্ভাষণ, কারণ-বিবরণ (জ্ঞান বৃদ্ধি, শব্দভাণ্ডার উন্নয়ন, সাম্প্রতিক ঘটনার অবগতিও সমালোচনামূলক চিন্তা) এবং বন্ধুত্বপূর্ণ উপদেশ থাকে। এই গঠন ও টোন পাঠককে বোঝাতে ও নিয়মিত অভ্যাস গঠনে কার্যকরভাবে সাহায্য করে।

Question:
Suppose you are Shamim, Rifat is your younger brother. Write an e-mail to your younger brother advising him to take part in games and sports regularly.

Subject: Embrace the Joy of Sports: A Message for Rifat

Hey Rifat,

I hope this email finds you in good health and high spirits. I wanted to share some thoughts with you about the wonderful world of games and sports. As your older brother, I believe that participating in sports can bring a lot of positivity and benefits to your life.

First and foremost, playing sports is a fantastic way to stay physically active. It helps you build strength, endurance, and flexibility, all of which contribute to a healthy lifestyle. Regular physical activity not only keeps your body fit but also boosts your immune system, ensuring you're better equipped to handle daily challenges.

Engaging in sports also has a positive impact on your mental well-being. It's a stress-buster that can lift your mood and reduce anxiety. The sense of accomplishment you get from improving your skills and achieving your goals on the field can do wonders for your self-esteem and confidence.

Moreover, participating in team sports teaches you valuable life lessons. You learn the importance of teamwork, communication, and collaboration. You'll discover how to handle victories graciously and cope with defeats gracefully, which are essential skills in all aspects of life.

Sports also provide an excellent opportunity to make new friends and expand your social circle. When you're part of a team, you're surrounded by like-minded individuals who share your passion. These friendships can last a lifetime and enrich your overall life experience.

Lastly, participating in sports can help you develop discipline and time management skills. Balancing your studies, hobbies, and sports activities teaches you how to manage your time effectively, a skill that will serve you well in the future.

So, Rifat, consider taking part in games and sports regularly. Whether it's soccer, cricket, basketball, or any other activity you enjoy, embrace it wholeheartedly. It's not just about winning or competing; it's about the joy of playing, staying healthy, and growing as an individual.

Take care and have a blast on the field!

Shamim

Question #80 (ID: 209153)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, your younger brother Kamal is an HSC Examinee. Now, write an e-mail telling him to study seriously to be well prepared for the ensuing examiantion.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To :

Subject: Your Success Lies in Your Preparation: Time to Study Seriously!

Hey Kamal,

I hope this email finds you in good health and high spirits. With the HSC examinations just around the corner, I wanted to have a heart-to-heart talk about the importance of serious preparation.

I know you've got a lot on your plate right now, and the pressure might be building up. But remember, the key to success in any examination lies in your preparation. Here are a few reasons why studying seriously is crucial:

Strong Foundation: The concepts you grasp during your study sessions create a strong foundation for your understanding of the subjects. A solid base will help you tackle even the trickiest questions with confidence.

Time Management: Serious study habits will help you manage your time effectively. Break your study sessions into manageable chunks and allocate sufficient time to each subject. This will prevent last-minute cramming and reduce stress.

Reduced Anxiety: Proper preparation helps alleviate anxiety. When you've covered the syllabus thoroughly, you'll enter the examination hall with a sense of calmness and assurance.

Concept Clarity: Serious studying ensures you truly understand the topics instead of just memorizing them. This will enable you to answer questions creatively and thoughtfully, impressing the examiners.

Achieve Your Goals: Your dedication and hard work during these crucial months can make a significant impact on your results. Visualize your goals and remind yourself of the rewards that await your success.

Confidence Boost: The more you study, the more confident you become in your abilities. Confidence is a key ingredient for success, both in exams and in life.

I understand that distractions can be tempting, and procrastination can sneak in. However, try to create a conducive study environment and set achievable goals for each day. Take short breaks to rejuvenate, but ensure that your study time is focused and productive.

Remember, your family, friends, and teachers are all here to support you. If you're facing challenges in any subject, don't hesitate to ask for help. Everyone wants to see you succeed.

Believe in yourself, Kamal. Your potential is limitless, and these exams are just a stepping stone toward your dreams. Study seriously, stay focused, and give it your best shot. We're all rooting for your success!

Wishing you strength, determination, and the will to conquer every challenge.

Best regards,

[Your Name]

Explanation:
This message is appropriate because it combines a caring, encouraging tone with specific, actionable advice (study schedule, revision methods, and rest) that makes preparation practical and motivating. The underlying concept is that emotional support plus clear steps improves focus, consistency, and retention. Keep the email short, positive, and offer concrete help so Kamal feels supported and knows exactly what to do.

I know that you might worry, but please trust in my determination and efforts. I promise to give my all and make you proud. Your support and encouragement mean the world to me, and I want to assure you that I won't let you down.

In the meantime, I'll make sure to take short breaks to relax and recharge, so I can approach my studies with a clear mind and renewed energy.

Thank you for always being there for me, Mom. Your love and belief in me keep me motivated to excel. Let's keep our fingers crossed and look forward to the positive outcomes that my hard work will bring.

Take care, and I'll keep you updated on my progress.

With love and gratitude,

[Your Name]

Explanation:
সঠিক উত্তরটি মা’কে নিশ্চিন্ত করে কারণ এতে তুমি শান্ত স্বরে তোমার পড়াশোনার বর্তমান অগ্রগতি, নির্দিষ্ট প্রস্তুতির পরিকল্পনা এবং স্বাস্থ্যের অবস্থা স্পষ্টভাবে জানাবে। স্পষ্ট সময়সূচি ও অর্জিত প্রস্তুতির তথ্য দেওয়া এবং প্রয়োজন হলে সহায়তার অনুরোধ করা মায়ের উদ্বেগ কমায় এবং তার আস্থা বাড়ায়।
