Question #85 (ID: 209158)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Chittagong Board, Rajshahi Board, Barisal Board | Tags: Chattogram Board, Cumilla Board, Rajshahi Board, Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, you are Rafa. Write an email to your foreign friend narrating the scenic beauty of Bangladesh.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To : 

Subject: Discover the Enchanting Beauty of Bangladesh

Hey [Friend's Name],

I hope this email finds you in great spirits. I wanted to share with you the breathtaking beauty of my homeland, Bangladesh. I've been exploring its scenic landscapes lately, and I'm absolutely amazed by what this country has to offer.

Imagine lush green countryside stretching as far as the eye can see, adorned with emerald rice paddies that sway gently in the breeze. The rural landscapes here are like something out of a painting, with traditional huts dotting the fields and locals going about their daily lives with warm smiles.

One of the most enchanting sights I've come across is the Sundarbans, the world's largest mangrove forest that spreads across the delta. Towering trees emerge from the water, forming a labyrinth of waterways and small islands. The tranquillity of this place is simply mesmerising, especially during sunrise and sunset when the golden hues create a magical ambiance.

The tea gardens in Sylhet are another marvel. Rows upon rows of tea bushes cover the rolling hills, presenting a soothing gradient of greens. Taking a stroll through these gardens while sipping on freshly brewed tea is an experience that soothes the soul.

Bangladesh is also home to a multitude of rivers, and the beauty of river life is an integral part of our culture. Watching fishermen casting their nets, ferries slowly gliding across the water, and vibrant boats reflecting in the river's mirror-like surface is truly captivating. The Padma, Meghna, and Jamuna rivers are just a few examples of the life-giving arteries that weave through the land.

And let's not forget the ancient city of Bagerhat with its stunning UNESCO-listed mosque complexes. The Sixty Dome Mosque, in particular, is an architectural marvel that stands as a testament to our rich history.

The cultural diversity of Bangladesh is yet another facet to admire. Festivals like Pohela Boishakh (Bengali New Year) and Durga Puja are celebrated with immense joy and vibrancy, bringing people together in a riot of colors and traditions.

I wish you could join me in person to witness the splendor of Bangladesh. The sights, sounds, and flavors are unlike anything you've experienced before. Perhaps, someday, you'll get a chance to visit and explore it all with me.

Looking forward to hearing from you soon and catching up on everything. Take care!

Warm regards,

Rafa

Explanation:
The correct answer is an email written in Rafa’s voice that directly addresses a foreign friend and uses vivid, sensory descriptions and specific examples (like the Sundarbans, tea gardens, rivers and paddy fields) to portray Bangladesh’s scenic beauty. This is appropriate because it follows the task (narration by Rafa) and demonstrates how to use first-person perspective, concrete images, and a warm tone to make a place come alive. Keeping sentences simple and including place names and personal feelings helps readers understand and visualize the scenery.

Over the past few months, I've been focusing heavily on my studies, setting a well-structured routine that covers all subjects comprehensively. Creating a study timetable has been a game-changer for me; it helps me allocate sufficient time to each subject while maintaining a balance so I don't feel overwhelmed.

One of the strategies I've found most effective is practising with past exam papers and sample questions. It not only familiarises me with the exam pattern but also helps me gauge my strengths and weaknesses. This way, I can concentrate on improving the areas where I need more work.

I hope you're also doing well and finding effective ways to prepare. Let's keep cheering each other on as we approach this milestone in our academic journey.

Looking forward to catching up soon. Take care and stay focused!

Warm regards,

[Your Name]

Explanation:
The email is correct because it clearly describes concrete steps—study schedule, materials used, practice with past papers, and revision techniques—so your friend can see exactly how you prepared rather than just hearing vague statements. Subject: Inquiry about Admission Procedure for Overseas Students

Dear Graduate Admissions,

[Your Name]

Question #91 (ID: 209091)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the following story and complete it in your own way. Give a suitable title to the story:

There was a naughty cowboy who grazed his cows beside a forest. He used to make fun with people crying Tiger! Tiger!....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Liar Cowboy

There was a naughty cowboy who grazed his cows beside a forest. He used to make fun with people crying Tiger! Tiger! Help! Help!" The villagers heard his cry and ran to help him. When they came near him, they found no tiger there and the boy laughed at them. The villagers were fooled by the cunning boy and hence, they went away. After a few days, he made the same fun and the villagers came again to help him but found no tiger there. One day, a tiger really came and it attacked the cattle. The boy somehow climbed up a tree and shouted for help. The villagers heard him but they thought that he was kidding again and so, no one came to help him. The tiger killed one of his cows and took it away. The boy felt sorry for his silly joke. From then, he promised not to tell a lie and befool people again.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: কাহিনির শুরুতে কৌতুকপ্রিয় গৃহপালকের বারবার অযথা 'বাঘ!' চেঁচানো তার আচরণ ও পরিণতি সম্পর্কে আগাম ইঙ্গিত দেয়, তাই এমন একটি সমাপ্তি — যেখানে সত্যিকারের বিপদে লোকেরা আর তাকে বিশ্বাস করে না এবং সে শিক্ষা পায় — যুক্তিযুক্ত ও উপযুক্ত। এই শেষাংশে কারণে-প্রতিক্রিয়ার স্পষ্টতা, চরিত্র পরিবর্তন ও নৈতিক শিক্ষা রয়েছে, যা গল্পকে সঙ্গত ও অর্থবহ করে তুলে।

Question #92 (ID: 209092)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

There lived a happy cobbler who passed his days working and singing from morning till night. A rich neighbour of his was a banker who one day said to him, "How much a year do you earn?"........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Obsession with Money

Once, there lived a happy cobbler in a town. He passed his days in singing and dancing. A rich neighbour of his was a banker. One day, the banker said to him, "How much a year do you earn?" The cobbler smiled and said, "I do not know, sir. I have never counted in that way, as I live from hand to mouth. Everyday I earn and I buy my meal with that income and return home. I cannot save any money from my income. Despite this, I am happy." Then, the banker said, "I have decided to get rid you of poverty. Take this ten thousand taka, preserve them carefully and use them in time of want." The cobbler who had never seen so much money at a time in his life before got startled, and came back home quickly. After returning home, he was restless as he could not find any safe place to hide the money. At last, he dug a hole inside his room and hid the money in it. At night, he was unable to sleep as he was obsessed with the money. He would remain alert the successive few nights. Thus, he lost his sleep and| happiness. One day, he went to the banker and told mental peace. So, he requested the banker to take his | him that his money had snatched away his sleep and money back. Finally, the cobbler gave the money to the banker. Now, he was able to enjoy sound sleep as before.

Explanation:
A fitting completion shows the cobbler answering that he earns just enough and is happy, which directly answers the banker's question while preserving the cheerful tone and resolving the conflict. This works because the story uses contrast between wealth and contentment to teach that happiness depends on attitude, not money, conveyed through simple dialogue and character action.

Question #93 (ID: 209093)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

Bithi is a shelterless, helpless street orphan of ten years who sells flowers on the intersection of Dhaka street. She lives on the income of what she gets from selling flowers. One day, while selling flowers in the traffic jam..............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Bithi- A Good Hearted Street Orphan

Bithi is a shelterless, helpless street orphan of ten years who sells flowers on the intersections of Dhaka street. She lives on the income of what she gets from selling flowers. One day, while selling flowers in the traffic jam, she saw a foreign lady walking on the nearby footpath. Bithi noticed that the lady was not feeling well. Within a few seconds, the lady fell on the ground. So, she ran to the unconscious lady. In the meantime, the signal turned green and all the vehicles started moving. That's why Bithi found none to call for help and she got really puzzled. She thought for a moment and sprinkled some water on the lady's face and tried to wake her up. The lady opened her eyes, tried to say something but she failed to say anything. Then Bithi stopped a rickshaw puller and requested to help her. After that, they took her to the nearby hospital. Though the rickshaw puller left, Bithi stayed there. The duty doctors started the procedure. After a while, they took the lady out of the emergency for treatment. Before losing her sense again, last thing she noticed was a sad and tensed face of a little girl.

Bithi came out of the hospital but she could not forget the incident. She became busy in her regular life. Still, she remembers the foreign lady, her blank look, both of their helplessness now and then. A few months later, while selling flowers in the same location the incident took place, she notices a mini crowd of the street children on the footpath. She also goes there to find out what is happening. After going there, with utter surprise, Bithi finds out that the same lady is searching someone in the crowd. When the lady notices Bithi, she comes to her and hugs her really tight. After this meeting, everything changes in Bithi's life. The lady takes her to a place where there are so many children like her. They study there and and also get trained for different things. Now, Bithi does not have to worry about her shelter, food or any of the basic needs. Moreover, everyone is very affectionate to her. The lady also visits her very often. She has introduced Bithi to her family as well. Bithi likes them very much. Now she does not feel lonely anymore and she knows the feeling to be loved and cared.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: গল্পের সঠিক পরিণতি সেইসব ঘটনা দেখায় যা বিথির অবস্থান ও রাস্তার পরিবেশ থেকে যুক্তিযুক্তভাবে উদ্ভব করে — যেমন যানজটের সময় কেউ তাকে ফুল কিনে সাহায্য করা বা কোনো দুর্ঘটনা/ঘটনা যা তার জীবনকে প্রভাবিত করে। এমন ধারা চরিত্রের কারণে-ফলের সম্পর্ক বজায় রেখে পাঠককে বিশ্বাসযোগ্যতা দেয় এবং চরিত্রের আবেগ ও পরিস্থিতি স্পষ্ট করে তোলে। সংক্ষিপ্ত, বাস্তবভিত্তিক বর্ণনা গল্পটিকে সুসংগত ও অর্থবহ করে তোলে।

Question #94 (ID: 209094)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

One day I was going to college to take my final exam at 10 am. At 9 when I was 20 minutes away from my college, suddenly a sick old man fell down...........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Helping Someone in Need

One day I was going to college to take my final exam at 10 am. At 9, when I was 20 minutes away from my college, suddenly a sick old man fell down. People ran to him. I saw him lying on the road. He was still breathing but was not responding. I was at a loss of what to do. I thought about running back home and getting help. Then someone there said that we should call an ambulance. I immediately called the national emergency service 999 to send for an ambulance. They instructed me to start doing CPR before the ambulance arrived.

By this time, he was hardly breathing, and only god knows when the ambulance would arrive. I had never done CPR in my life before, only watched people do it in the movies. I tried to do CPR on the man but it was harder than I imagined. You have to press with a great force and it was so scary to do as it may even break the ribcage.. After about ten minutes, the ambulance arrived. They rushed the man in. When the ambulance left, it was 9.50 a.m. already. I, then called the nearby rickshaw and hopped onto it. I reached the college at 10.15. The teachers did not like me being 15 minutes late for my final exam. I tried to explain what happened but they did not want to be bothered with a story. I was breathless when I started my exam as I came running towards the exam hall. I felt dizzy and lost. Then I calmed myself down, drank some water and started writing my answers. I was already 25 minutes late when I started writing. I, however, do not regret helping the old man in need as humanity always comes first to me. I would rather be late for helping a distressed person in need, than be on time for my exam, leaving the old man lying unattended on the road.

Explanation:
এই সমাপ্তিটি সঠিক কারণ এটি চরিত্রের নৈতিক সিদ্ধান্ত ও সময়গত টানকে পরিষ্কারভাবে তুলে ধরে—বৃদ্ধ লোকের প্রতি সাহায্য করার মানসিকতা এবং পরীক্ষায় দেরির সম্ভাব্য ফল একসঙ্গে দেখায়। গল্পের কারণ-ফল যুক্তি (বৃদ্ধ লোক পড়ে → সাহায্য করা বা না করা → পরীক্ষায় যাওয়ার সম্ভাব্যতা) পাঠককে ঘটনাগুলোর মধ্যকার সংযোগ বুঝতে সাহায্য করে। সংক্ষিপ্ত কিন্তু স্পষ্ট সংঘাত ও সমাধান থাকার কারণে পাঠক গল্পের উদ্দেশ্য ও নৈতিক পাঠ সহজে উপলব্ধি করতে পারে।

Question #95 (ID: 209095)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

Once a farmer had a goose. It used to lay a golden egg everyday. The farmer used to sell them in the local market and in no time he became quite solvent. But his wife was very greedy..................

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Grasp All Lose All

Once a farmer had a goose. It used to lay a golden egg everyday. The farmer used to sell them in the local market and in no time he became quite solvent. But his wife was very greedy.She thought that there were many eggs in the belly of the goose. She wanted to have all the eggs at a time to become rich overnight. One day, she hit upon a plan that she would cut the belly of the goose and get all the eggs of gold. She told her husband about her plan. Her husband, who was wise but not greedy, said to her, "Don't be greedy. Be happy with what we have." But the farmer's wife did not listen to him. She cut the belly of the goose with a sharp knife. But alas! She found no egg in it. Thus, the greedy wife lost his valuable goose.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: লোভে স্ত্রী হাঁসটিকে একবারে সব স্বর্ণ পাওয়ার আশায় মেরে ফেলেছিল, ফলে প্রতিদিন যে স্বর্ণের ডিম আসত তা হারিয়ে গেছে। এই কাহিনীর শিক্ষা—দীর্ঘমেয়াদী স্থিতিশীল লাভকে ধৈর্য দিয়ে রক্ষা করা উচিত; অল্প লাভের জন্য তা নাশ করা উচিত নয়।

Question #96 (ID: 209096)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

It was 20 March of 2020. Sarah was very happy because her family was going to have a tour to Saint Martin Island the next week. She was watching TV with a jolly mood. Suddenly, a news popped up "Government has declared lockdown for a period of 15 days all over the country with a view to controlling the spread of Covid-19 and protecting people from being infected with it....................

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adapting to Change: A Family's Experience in Lockdown

It was 20 March of 2020. Sarah was very happy because of her family was going to have a tour to Saint Martin Island the next week. She was watching TV with a jolly mood. Suddenly, a news popped up - "Government has declared lockdown for a period of 15 days all over the country with a view to controlling the spread of Covid-19 and protecting people from being infected with it. Sarah's face fell as she heard the news. Her family's trip to Saint Martin Island was now cancelled and they were going to be stuck at home for the next 15 days. She felt sad and disappointed but she also knew that the government's decision was necessary to protect people from the virus.

Sarah's family decided to make the best of the situation and use the time to bond and spend quality time together. They played board games, watched movies, and cooked meals together. Sarah was surprised at how much fun she was having with her family despite being stuck at home.

As the days went by, Sarah became more aware of the gravity of the situation. She saw the news reports of people falling ill and dying from the virus. She realized that the government's decision to lockdown the country was to protect people like her and her family from getting infected. She felt grateful to be safe at home with her loved ones and vowed to do her part in preventing the spread of the virus by staying at home and following the guidelines set by the government.

Sarah learned that sometimes difficult decisions have to be made for the greater good and that it's important to make the most of a bad situation. She also learned the importance of family and how much they mean to her. She was determined to cherish and appreciate the time she has with them even more in the future.

Explanation:
A good continuation ends with Sarah and her family responding realistically to the lockdown—canceling or postponing the trip, feeling disappointed, and then taking practical steps to stay safe. This is correct because it reflects the real consequences of a nationwide lockdown and shows characters adapting by following health rules, communicating, and finding alternative ways to enjoy time together. Such a continuation teaches responsibility, emotional resilience, and creates a clear, believable narrative arc.

Question #97 (ID: 209097)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

Once a golden necklace was lost from a richman's house. A few servants worked in that house. Naturally, it was suspected that any one of the servants had stolen the necklace.............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Wise Judge

Once a golden necklace was lost from a rich man's house. A few servants worked in that house. Naturally, it was suspected that any one of the servants had stolen the necklace. The rich man asked all of them but none of them confessed their guilt. So the rich man went to a judge. The judge was very wise. He called all the servants and asked them about the incident. All of them denied the charge. Then the judge hit upon a plan to find out the real thief. He gave each of them a stick of the same length and told them to return the sticks the next day. He told them that the stick of the real thief would increase by an inch. Returning home, all the servants kept their sticks as they were except the servant who stole the necklace. He shortened his stick by an inch. The next day when all the servants returned their sticks before the judge, the real thief was easily detected. Then the thief was given his due punishment.

Explanation:
সঠিক উত্তরটি কারণ গল্পে দেওয়া সূক্ষ্ম সূত্রগুলো—যেমন কাজের সময়ে কার অবস্থান, আলিবি ভাঙা, অথবা নেকলেসের কাছে পাওয়া কোনো ছোটো চিহ্ন—একজন নির্দিষ্ট চাকরির প্রতি নির্দেশ করে। মূল ধারণা হলো উপলব্ধ প্রমাণ ও সুযোগ বিশ্লেষণ করে যৌক্তিক সিদ্ধান্ত নেয়া; যখন আলিবি এবং প্রমাণ মিল করে তখন সেই সিদ্ধান্ত সত্য বলে ধরা যায়।

Question #98 (ID: 209098)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

Monon has studied Information and Communication Technology at a public university. He wants to be a skillful engineer. He is going to enter the job market and preparing himself accordingly. One day a company offers a job t Monon........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Monon's Struggle

Monon has studied Information and Communication Technology at a public university. He wants to be a skillful engineer. He is going to enter the job market and preparing himself accordingly. One day a company offers a job to Monon. He is over the moon to get a job offer so soon. He prepares himself for the job interview. On the day of the interview he got up early and got dressed nicely. The interview went well, but there was a fetch. At the end of the interview one of the interviewers indirectly asked him for bribe. He was shocked. They asked for a large amount of money that Monon could not afford. They told him to go home and think about it.

He went home heartbroken. His parents asked what happened and he explained everything. He was in a dilemma. He needed the job, but not at the cost of compromising his morality. Also, they could not afford to give away such a large sum of money. Monon felt like this country is full of corruption and there is no evaluation of talent. He felt like leaving the country and settling abroad. But he is the only child of his parents. So, leaving the country was really not an option for him. He decided to let go of that job offer and wait for other interview calls.

A month later, he got called for another interview. The interview went well, but he did not get called. Monon started to grow frustrated. He had applied to several companies but got interview calls from very few. He started having recurring thoughts of leaving the country for higher studies, but he was not able to leave his parents alone. He slowly started to fall into depression. A year later, he got another job offer. After doing some back and forth;he was finally able to land the job. He became hopeful about his life again and as he started to work, he began to slowly come out of depression. He was then able to help his parents financially which boosted his self-esteem. Monon realized that unemployment created depression in him and ruined his self-esteem. He promised himself that he would help the educated unemployed youths around him to get jobs and thus help them live their lives to the full potential.

Explanation:
Accepting the job makes sense because it gives Monon real-world experience to apply his ICT knowledge and build the practical skills needed to become a skillful engineer. He should confirm the role offers learning opportunities, mentorship, and room for growth so the job contributes to his career goals; if not, he can negotiate or keep searching while continuing to prepare.

Question #99 (ID: 209099)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

One day a boy of class five was going to school. Suddenly he saw a money bag on the road. He was at a loss...............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Honesty is the Best Policy: A Story of a Boy's Integrity

One day a boy of class five was going to school. Suddenly he saw a money bag on the road. He was at a loss. However, he quickly decided what to do. He walked to his school teacher's office and told her about the money bag he had found on the road. The teacher was impressed by his honesty and decided to help him return the money bag to its rightful owner. They opened the bag and found that it contained a large sum of money. The teacher contacted the local police and reported the find. After a few days, the police were able to track down the owner of the money bag, who was a local businessman. He had been on his way to the bank when he lost the bag. He was very grateful to the boy and the teacher for returning the money to him and he wanted to reward the boy for his honesty. The businessman gave the boy a generous reward and also offered him a scholarship for his education.

The boy felt proud of himself for doing the right thing and learned that honesty is the best policy. He realised that the reward he received for being honest was much greater than anything he could have gained by keeping the money for himself. He also learned that honesty is not only a moral virtue but also a practical one. He shared his experience with his classmates and encouraged them to always be honest and to do the right thing, even if it is difficult.

The whole school was proud of the boy's actions and the school principal even mentioned his story during the morning assembly. The boy was celebrated as an example of honesty and integrity. His story spread around the school and even the town and he became known as an example of honesty and integrity and a role model for other children.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ঘটনার সর্বোত্তম কাজ হলো টাকা ব্যাগটি তার মালিককে বা নিকটস্থ শিক্ষক/পুলিশের কাছে ফেরত দেওয়া, কারণ এটি সততা ও দায়িত্বশীলতার পরিচায়ক। সততা মানে অন্যদের অধিকার মেনে চলা ও নিজের সম্মান বজায় রাখা, যা দীর্ঘমেয়াদে বিশ্বাস ও শান্তির কারণ হয়।

Question #100 (ID: 209100)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once upon a time, a crow was very thirsty. It flew from place to place in search of water but unfortunately it did not find any water. All on a sudden it saw ………..

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Thirsty Crow/Necessity is the Mother of Invention

Once upon a time, a crow was very thirsty. It flew from place to place in search of water but unfortunately it did not find any water. All on a sudden, it saw a pitcher. It peeped into the pitcher and saw that there was a little wate at the bottom of the pitcher. It tried to drink some water but its bill could not reach the water. It tried again and again but in vain. It became very sad and hopeless. Suddenly, it saw some pebbles near the pitcher. A good idea came into its mind. The crow picked up the pebbles and dropped them into the pitcher one by one. As a result, the water came up to the brim. The crow then drank water from it to its heart's content and flew away with a joyful mind. Thus, its cleverness helped it satisfy its thirst.

Explanation:
The correct answer is "a pitcher (or pot) of water" because the thirsty crow, searching for water, would naturally see a vessel containing water; this matches the familiar fable "The Crow and the Pitcher," where the crow finds a pitcher of water and uses pebbles to drink.

Question #101 (ID: 209101)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board, Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board, Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once there lived a poor woodcutter. But he was very honest. He earned his livelihood by selling wood in the market. One day while he ………….

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
An Honest Woodcutter and a Beautiful Fairy

Once, there lived a poor woodcutter. But he was very honest. He earned his livelihood by selling wood in the market. One day, while he was cutting wood near a pond, suddenly, his axe fell into the pond. The pond was very deep. The woodcutter did not know how to swim or dive. So, he was sitting there sadly. Then a wonderful thing happened. A beautiful fairy appeared before the woodcutter. She asked him in a sweet voice, "Why are you so sad? Why are you not cutting wood?" The woodcutter replied sorrowfully, "My axe has fallen into the pond. I can't cut wood now." The fairy then showed him an axe made of silver and asked him if it was his axe. The woodcutter saw the axe and said, "It's not my axe." The fairy showed him another axe made of gold and asked, "Is this the axe that you lost?" The woodcutter said, "No, it's not. My axe is made of iron. It was old." The fairy showed him the lost axe with a wooden handle. The woodcutter then said happily that it was his axe. The fairy became very pleased and gave him the golden and the silver axes too as a reward of his honesty. The wood cutter became very happy getting the axes made of golden and silver. He thanked the fairy and went home. Later, selling those two axes in the market, he made quite a good amount of money. He became solvent and started passing his days happily ever after. Thus, the honest people are rewarded everywhere for their honesty.

Explanation:
Explanation: The correct answer is "was cutting wood near the river" because the past continuous tense describes an action that was in progress at a particular time and sets the scene for what follows (for example, his axe slipping into the water). Using past continuous is natural here to show an ongoing activity that gets interrupted by the next event in the story.

Question #102 (ID: 209102)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board, Dinajpur Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

It was a bright sunny morning I was going to college with some of my friends. We were in a hilarious mood as we were talking about our plan to go on a picnic. Suddenly….

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Privileged Should Extend Helping Hands to the Poor

It was a bright sunny morning. I was going to college with some of my friends. We were in a hilarious mood as we were talking about our plan to go on a picnic. Suddenly, we noticed an old woman who was begging money for her ailing son. It was hard for us to turn a blind eye. Her torn clothes and sad face brought tears to our eyes and we decided to help her. When we asked her about her son, she replied that her son was a garments worker and had been crippled due to an accident in the factory. The owner did not provide any compensation, and since then, she had to beg for buying foods and medicine for her son. All of us felt sorrow for the unfortunate woman and gave her the money we saved for the picnic. Then, we again started for the college while thanking the Almighty about our privileged lives. We have our health, a roof over our head, foods on table and a million other blessings to count. It is the duty of the wealthy and the privileged section of the society to come forward to aid these unfortunate people.

Explanation:
Explanation: The continuation that follows a sudden, unexpected event is correct because the word "Suddenly…" signals a shift from a relaxed scene to a conflict or surprise, so the story should introduce an incident that disrupts the picnic plan. This uses the basic storytelling principle of cause-and-effect—an unexpected event provokes characters' reactions and drives the plot forward. Keep sensory details and characters' responses clear to make the turn believable and engaging.

Ans.

An Honest Woodcutter and a Beautiful Fairy Once, there lived a woodcutter. He was very poor but honest. He lived on the bank of a river near a jungle. He used to cut wood to earn his living. One day, he was cutting wood near a pond. Suddenly, his axe fell into the pond. The pond was very deep. The woodcutter did not know how to swim or dive. So, he was sitting there sadly. The woodcutter replied sorrowfully, "My axe has fallen into the pond. I can't cut wood now." The fairy then showed him an axe made of silver and asked him if it was his axe. One day a boy of class five was going to school. Suddenly, he saw a money bag on the road. He was at a loss…

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Honesty is the Best Policy: A Story of a Boy's Integrity

One day a boy of class five was going to school. Suddenly he saw a money bag on the road. He was at a loss. However, he quickly decided what to do. He walked to his school teacher's office and told her about the money bag he had found on the road. The teacher was impressed by his honesty and decided to help him return the money bag to its rightful owner. They opened the bag and found that it contained a large sum of money. The teacher contacted the local police and reported the find. After a few days, the police were able to track down the owner of the money bag, who was a local businessman. Question #105 (ID: 209105)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once there lived a poor farmer. He had a goose. It used to lay a golden egg every day. He sold the golden egg in the market. He was very greedy …..

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Greedy Farmer/Grasp All Lose All

Once there lived a poor farmer. He had a goose. It used to lay a golden egg every day. He sold the golden egg in the market. He was very greedy. He thought that there were many eggs in the belly of the goose. He wanted to have all the eggs at a time to become rich overnight. One day, he hit upon a plan that he would cut the belly of the goose and get all the eggs of gold. He told his wife about his plan. His wife, who was wise but not greedy, said to her husband, "Don't be greedy. Be happy with what we have." But the farmer did not listen to her. He cut the belly of the goose with a sharp knife. But alas! He found no egg in it. Thus, the greedy farmer lost his valuable goose.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: কৃষক লোভের ফলশ্রুতিতে এককালীন বেশি সোনা পেতে হাঁসটিকে নষ্ট করে ফেলল, ফলে নিয়মিত সোনার ডিমের উৎস টিকে না থাকা কারণে আর ডিম পাওয়া গেল না। মূল ধারণা: স্বল্পমেয়াদী লাভের লোভে স্থায়ী ও নিয়মিত সুবিধা ধ্বংস করলে শেষ পর্যন্ত নিজের ক্ষতি হয়; ধৈর্য ও টেকসই উপার্জন বেশি লাভজনক।

Question:
Parul was a school girl whose parents were landless. They were unable to bear her educational expenses. But Parul was determined. ……………

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Where There Is a Will, There Is a Way

Parul was a school girl whose parents were landless. They were unable to bear her educational expenses. But Parul was determined to complete her studies. In her class, she was the best student. Her teachers always encouraged her to do better in school. However, she could not afford to attend classes regularly as she had to help her parents in their daily chores. Moreover, she tutored a few students in the evening in order to bear a minimum academic expenses. One day, one of her teachers found her sobbing at the corner of her classroom. He gently asked her, "What's wrong, Parul?" Hearing his voice, Parul was a bit startled and answered, "Nothing Sir, I am fine." The teacher, however, insisted to know if he could help her in any way. He promptly spoke to the headmaster concerning her situation and managed to offer her a waiver for the registration fee. Question:
happy cobbler in a town. He passed his days in singing and dancing…....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Obsession with Money

Once, there lived a happy cobbler in a town. He passed his days in singing and dancing. A rich neighbour of his was a banker. One day, the banker said to him, "How much a year do you earn?" The cobbler smiled and said, "I do not know, sir. I have never counted in that way, as I live from hand to mouth. Everyday I earn and I buy my meal with that income and return home. I cannot save any money from my income. Despite this, I am happy." Then, the banker said, "I have decided to get rid you of poverty. Take this ten thousand taka, preserve them carefully and use them in time of want." The cobbler who had never seen so much money at a time in his life before got startled, and came back home quickly. After returning home, he was restless as he could not find any safe place to hide the money. At last, he dug a hole inside his room and hid the money in it. At night, he was unable to sleep as he was obsessed with the money. He would remain alert the successive few nights. Thus, he lost his sleep and| happiness. One day, he went to the banker and told mental peace. So, he requested the banker to take his | him that his money had snatched away his sleep and money back. Finally, the cobbler gave the money to the banker. Now, he was able to enjoy sound sleep as before.

Explanation:
Explanation: The phrase "passed his days in singing and dancing" is correct because "in" is followed by gerund verbs ("singing," "dancing") that name activities, and the whole phrase means he "spent his time" doing those activities. This uses the idiom "pass one’s days in + -ing" to show a habitual or continuous way of living.

Question #110 (ID: 209110)

Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once a crow was sitting on the branch of a tree. It had a piece of meat in its beak. Suddenly a fox came there ......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Sly Fox and a Foolish Crow

Once, a crow was sitting on the branch of a tree. It had a piece of meat in its beak. Suddenly, a fox came there. When he came under that tree, he noticed the meat in the crow's beak. The sight of the piece of meat made his mouth filled with water. He thought for sometimes. Then, he hit upon a plan to have it. He said to the crow, "Oh beautiful crow! Your complexion is so fair. I think, you can sing nicely. Would you please sing a song for me?" At first, the crow did not want to sing. But as the fox carried on praising her, she felt proud of her tongue. Finally, she started to sing a song. But no sooner had she opened her mouth than the piece of meat fell off her mouth. In the meantime, the clever fox took it and ran away. The crow had paid a heavy price for her foolishness.

Explanation:
The fox praised the crow to make it proud, so the crow opened its beak to sing and dropped the meat, which the fox then took — that explains why the fox succeeded. The lesson is that flattery can trick people into foolish actions, so don’t let pride or desire for praise override common sense.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
One day, a girl of class five was going to school. Suddenly, she saw a money bag dropped by someone on the road. She was at a loss ….....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Honesty is the Best Policy: A Story of a Girl's Integrity

One day a girl of class five was going to school. Suddenly she saw a money bag on the road. She was at a loss. However, She quickly decided what to do. She walked to her school teacher's office and told her about the money bag she had found on the road. The teacher was impressed by her honesty and decided to help him return the money bag to its rightful owner. They opened the bag and found that it contained a large sum of money. The teacher contacted the local police and reported the find. After a few days, the police were able to track down the owner of the money bag, who was a local businessman. He had been on his way to the bank when he lost the bag. He was very grateful to the girl and the teacher for returning the money to him and he wanted to reward the girl for her honesty. The businessman gave the girl a generous reward and also offered him a scholarship for her education.

The girl felt proud of herself for doing the right thing and learned that honesty is the best policy. She realised that the reward she received for being honest was much greater than anything she could have gained by keeping the money for herself. She also learned that honesty is not only a moral virtue but also a practical one. She shared her experience with her classmates and encouraged them to always be honest and to do the right thing, even if it is difficult.

The whole school was proud of the girl's actions and the school principal even mentioned his story during the morning assembly. The girl was celebrated as an example of honesty and integrity. Her story spread around the school and even the town and she became known as an example of honesty and integrity and a role model for other children.

Explanation:
সঠিক সিদ্ধান্ত হল ব্যাগের টাকা কোনোভাবে মালিকের কাছে পৌঁছে দেওয়া বা স্কুলের শিক্ষক/পুলিশকে জানানো, কারণ সেটি সততা ও দায়বোধ দেখায় এবং অন্যকে ক্ষতি থেকে রক্ষা করে। এই বিষয়টি শেখায় যে অন্যের জিনিস খুঁজে পেলে সেটি নিজের হিসেবে নেওয়ার পরিবর্তে ফেরত দেওয়াই নৈতিক ও সামাজিকভাবে সঠিক কাজ।

Question:
Once an ant was very thirsty. He went to a river to drink water. When he began to drink water, a wave ......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
An Ant and a Dove Once

Once, an ant was very thirsty. He went to a river to drink water. When he began to drink water, a wave swept him away. He was about to drown. There was a tree on the bank of the river and a dove was sitting on a branch of it. She noticed that the ant was about to drown. Feeling pity for the ant, the dove wanted to save him. So, she dropped a leaf in front of the ant. The ant got on the leaf and the dove took the leaf on the bank of the river. Thus the dove saved the ant's life. Being grateful, the ant thanked her a lot. Another day, when the ant was seeking food under that tree, he noticed that a hunter was aiming at the dove. The dove did not notice it. The ant thought, "I must save the life of the dove as she saved mine the other day". So, he bit on the right leg of the hunter. At this the hunter's hands trembled and the bullet missed its aim. Then, the dove flew away and was saved.

Explanation:
Explanation: "Washed him away" is correct because a moving wave exerts a force on small objects and carries them along, so the ant would be carried off by the water. In a past-tense narrative we use the past simple verb "washed" to describe that completed action.

Correct Answer:

A Thirsty Crow

Once upon a time, a crow became very thirsty. It was summer and the weather was very hot. There was little water in that place. The crow flew here and there looking for water. But it could not find water anywhere. It seems that it was about to die for the thirst of water. But it did not lose heart.

The crow continued its search and found a pitcher to drink water. But there was a little water at the bottom of the pitcher. The crow tried to drink but failed. After dropping a number of stones, the water level in the jar roses high enough to reach. Then, the crow drank water. Thus the crow saved his life by the use of his wisdom.

A Sly Fox and a Foolish Crow

The sight of the piece of meat made his mouth filled with water. He thought for a moment. Then he hit upon a plan to have it. He said to the crow, "Oh beautiful Crow! Your complexion is so fair. Pranks are not Always Fun

It was late at night. I was taking preparation for my ensuing examination. All the members of my family were sleeping. All on a sudden, my phone rang and it was an unknown number. I got frightened because late night phone calls either mean an emergency or something scary to me. My father was out on an official tour and suddenly it came to my mind that something might have happened to him. I received the call and asked who it was. No one replied but I heard that someone heaved a deep sigh. It made me more scared and I repeated the same question. But the result was same; no one replied. There was a naughty cowboy who grazed his cows beside a forest. He used to make fun with people crying Tiger! Tiger! ………..

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Liar Cowboy

There was a naughty cowboy who grazed his cows beside a forest. He used to make fun with people crying Tiger! Tiger! Help! Help!" The villagers heard his cry and ran to help him. When they came near him, they found no tiger there and the boy laughed at them. The villagers were fooled by the cunning boy and hence, they went away. After a few days, he made the same fun and the villagers came again to help him but found no tiger there. One day, a tiger really came and it attacked the cattle. The boy somehow climbed up a tree and shouted for help. The villagers heard him but they thought that he was kidding again and so, no one came to help him. The tiger killed one of his cows and took it away. The boy felt sorry for his silly joke. From then, he promised not to tell a lie and befool people again.

Explanation:
Because he kept shouting "Tiger!" as a joke when there was no danger, people stopped believing him and ignored his warnings when real danger came. The underlying idea is that lying destroys trust, so false alarms make genuine warnings ineffective.

Question #118 (ID: 209118)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
There was a boy who hailed from an obscure background. But he was brilliant, diligent and innovative. He …...

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Innovation of the Innovative Boy

There was a boy who hailed from an obscure background. But he was brilliant, diligent and innovative. He belonged to a village where there was no electricity. During summer, the atmosphere of the village was hot and humid. The villagers were even suffering from the high temperature at home. They were becoming sick due to hot weather. Some of them even died of heat stroke. The boy, however, was thinking of an idea how to get rid of the heat. He came to know from a physics teacher of his school that the gas cools when it expands quickly. So, he thought of making an air cooler out of plastic bottles for his own house. So, he collected some plastic bottles and cut them into half. Then, he mounted them on a board. After that, he placed the board over a window, with the bottlenecks facing towards the inner side of the house. As a result, the change in pressure that occurred when air entered the wider part of the bottle and came out through the bottleneck cooled the air. That's how he successfully made the air cooler out of the plastic bottles. When the villagers found it effective, they requested the boy to make the cooler for them too. As the raw plastic bottles were easily available, the cooler could be made easily and it was cheap as well. In this way, the boy could reduce the sufferings of the village and also earn some money.

Explanation:
Explanation: The best completion is a phrase like "made a name for himself" (or "rose to prominence") because the contrast introduced by "But" and the qualities "brilliant, diligent and innovative" imply a resulting rise to recognition or success. In sentence completion, choose a continuation that logically follows from the prior information—here, his talents explain why someone from an obscure background would become well known.

Question #119 (ID: 209076)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board, Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board, Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once there lived a poor woodcutter. But he was very honest. He earned his livelihood by selling wood in the market. One day while he ………….

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
An Honest Woodcutter and a Beautiful Fairy

Once, there lived a poor woodcutter. But he was very honest. He earned his livelihood by selling wood in the market. One day, while he was cutting wood near a pond, suddenly, his axe fell into the pond. The pond was very deep. The woodcutter did not know how to swim or dive. So, he was sitting there sadly. Then a wonderful thing happened. A beautiful fairy appeared before the woodcutter. She asked him in a sweet voice, "Why are you so sad? Why are you not cutting wood?" The woodcutter replied sorrowfully, "My axe has fallen into the pond. I can't cut wood now." The fairy then showed him an axe made of silver and asked him if it was his axe. The woodcutter saw the axe and said, "It's not my axe." The fairy showed him another axe made of gold and asked, "Is this the axe that you lost?" The woodcutter said, "No, it's not. My axe is made of iron. It was old." The fairy showed him the lost axe with a wooden handle. The woodcutter then said happily that it was his axe. The fairy became very pleased and gave him the golden and the silver axes too as a reward of his honesty. The wood cutter became very happy getting the axes made of golden and silver. He thanked the fairy and went home. Later, selling those two axes in the market, he made quite a good amount of money. He became solvent and started passing his days happily ever after. Thus, the honest people are rewarded everywhere for their honesty.

Explanation:
The correct answer ("was cutting wood in the forest") fits because the passage says he earned his living by selling wood, so his likely activity at that moment is cutting wood. Use context clues and coherence—choose the option that logically follows the character's occupation and leads naturally into the next events of the story.

Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

It was a bright sunny morning I was going to college with some of my friends. We were in a hilarious mood as we were talking about our plan to go on a picnic. Suddenly….

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Privileged Should Extend Helping Hands to the Poor

It was a bright sunny morning. I was going to college with some of my friends. We were in a hilarious mood as we were talking about our plan to go on a picnic. Suddenly, we noticed an old woman who was begging money for her ailing son. It was hard for us to turn a blind eye. Her torn clothes and sad face brought tears to our eyes and we decided to help her. When we asked her about her son, she replied that her son was a garments worker and had been crippled due to an accident in the factory. The owner did not provide any compensation, and since then, she had to beg for buying foods and medicine for her son. All of us felt sorrow for the unfortunate woman and gave her the money we saved for the picnic. Then, we again started for the college while thanking the Almighty about our privileged lives. We have our health, a roof over our head, foods on table and a million other blessings to count. It is the duty of the wealthy and the privileged section of the society to come forward to aid these unfortunate people.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এই সম্পূরক অংশটি সঠিক কারণ এটি গল্পের শুরুতে নির্মিত কৌতুকপূর্ণ মেজাজ বজায় রেখে হঠাৎ ঘটনার মাধ্যমে উত্তেজনা বা সংঘাত যোগ করে পাঠকের আগ্রহ বাড়ায়। এর ন্যারেটিভ যৌক্তিক — চরিত্রদের প্রতিক্রিয়া, ঘটনা ও ফলাফল পরস্পরের সাথে সংযুক্ত আছে, তাই গল্পের উত্তরণ স্বচ্ছ এবং বিশ্বাসযোগ্য থাকে। মূল ধারণা হলো গল্পে ধারাবাহিকতা, কারণ-ফল সূত্র এবং জীবন্ত বর্ণনার মাধ্যমে পাঠককে সংযুক্ত রাখা।

Question #121 (ID: 209078)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story.

There was a pond full of frogs. Some of them often put their heads out of the water and croaked loudly. One day, some boys were playing by the side of the pond. When they heard the frogs croaking.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Naughty Boys and the Frogs

There was an old pond in a village. It was full of frogs. The frogs were living happily there. Some of them often put their heads out of the water and croaked loudly. One day, some boys were playing by the side of the pond. When they heard the frogs croaking, they started throwing stones at the frogs and made fun. The stone hit the frogs. As a result, some frogs were killed and many were wounded. The frogs were very much puzzled and did not know what to do. At last, an old frog raised its head and said, "Dear little boys, why are you killing us?" The boys said, "We are not killing you. We are just playing." Then the frog said, "What is play to you is death to us." The boys became very sorry and ashamed. So, they stopped their game and left the place.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এই উত্তরটি সঠিক কারণ তা গল্পের শুরু থেকেই যুক্তিযুক্তভাবে এগোয় — বাঁচচেগুলো ব্যাঙ্গ করে কেঁকড়ে এবং তাদের শুনে বাচ্চাদের প্রতিক্রিয়া দেখানো হয়েছে, ফলে কাহিনীর ক্রমধারা বজায় থাকে। ভাল সম্পূরক অংশগুলোতে কারণ‑প্রভাব, চরিত্রের কাজ ও প্রতিক্রিয়া, এবং একটি পরিষ্কার ফলাফল বা শিক্ষা থাকে; এগুলোই গল্পকে সম্পূর্ণ ও বোধগম্য করে।

Question #122 (ID: 209079)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

Once on a summer day, the scorching heat of the sun induced a Lion and a Boar to come at the same moment to a small well to drink. They fiercely disputed which of them should drink first, and were soon engaged in.....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

The Two Fight, The Third Benefits

Once on a summer day, the scorching heat of the sun induced a Lion and a Boar to come at the same moment to a small well to drink. They fiercely disputed which of them should drink first, and were soon engaged in the agonies of a mortal combat. They attacked each other with the utmost fury. It seemed that the fight would not be ceased until or unless one of them was dead. However, when they stopped to catch their breath for a fiercer renewal of the fight, they saw some vultures seated on a rock above evidently waiting for one of them or both to be killed. Then those vultures would fly down to feast on the carcase. The sight sobered them at once, and they came to realize that unnecessary fight would bring misery only for themselves. They at once made up their quarrel, saying, “It is better for us to make friends, than to become the food of Crows or Vultures.”

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: উক্ত কাহিনীর ধারায় "তারা তীব্রভাবে লড়াইয়ে লিপ্ত হলো"—এটিই সঠিক সমাপ্তি, কারণ উভয়েই একই সীমিত পানির উৎসকে নিজের অধিকার মনে করে গর্ব ও লোভের কারণে সংঘর্ষে জড়ায়। এই শেষ করুনটি মূল ধারণা পরিষ্কার করে—সীমিত সম্পদ ও অহংকারের ফলস্বরূপ দ্বন্দ্ব এবং সেই দ্বন্দ্বে উভয়েরই ক্ষতি হতে পারার নৈতিক শিক্ষা।

Question #123 (ID: 209080)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

Once, there was a selfish giant who had a large and beautiful garden. The garden was full of soft green grass. Here and there all over the grass stood many colourful flowers like stars.......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

Selfishness to Kindness

Once, there was a selfish giant who had a large and beautiful garden. The garden was full of soft green grass. Here and there all over the grass stood many colourful flowers like stars. The garden was a playground for the beautiful children. The children used to like the garden very much. So, they came to the garden every day to play different kinds of games. But they did not know that the selfish giant was the owner of the garden. They came and played as usual. Suddenly the giant noticed the children playing in his garden. Then he planned to make a big wall so that they could not enter the garden. Ultimately he made a big wall. As a result, the children coming near the garden could not enter into it. In the meantime, the garden had been flowerless and grass less. It was losing its beauty gradually. The selfish giant thought himself of the matter. At this he got into a great tension and tried to find out the real cause behind it. At last, he realized his mistakes and said to himself, - "Children are the great blessings of the garden". He called the children, made a good relationship with them and loved them from his core of heart. He allowed them to enter the garden and play again. Then the garden started to get back its beauty slowly. And eventually, it became the same as like as it was before. Thus, the selfish giant gained self-knowledge and self-realization through his mistakes.

Explanation:
Explanation: Completing the story by showing the giant’s change from selfishness to kindness is right because it follows the setup—the beautiful garden and the giant’s cruelty create a clear contrast that invites a moral resolution. This teaches the concept of character development and cause-and-effect: selfish actions bring loneliness or “winter,” while generosity restores warmth and life. Keeping the garden and children as symbols helps readers understand the lesson about compassion and the rewards of sharing.

Question #124 (ID: 209081)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board, Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board, Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the following story and complete it in your own way. Give a title to it.

Once, there lived a woodcutter. He was very poor but honest. He lived on the bank of a river near a jungle. He used to cut wood....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

An Honest Woodcutter and a Beautiful Fairy Once, there lived a woodcutter. He was very poor but honest. He lived on the bank of a river near a jungle. He used to cut wood to earn his living. One day, he was cutting wood near a pond. Suddenly, his axe fell into the pond. The pond was very deep. The woodcutter did not know how to swim or dive. So, he was sitting there sadly. Then, a wonderful thing happened. A beautiful fairy appeared before the woodcutter. She asked him in a sweet voice, "Why are you so sad? Why are you not cutting wood?" The woodcutter replied sorrowfully, "My axe has fallen into the pond. I can't cut wood now." The fairy then showed him an axe made of silver and asked him if it was his axe. The woodcutter saw the axe and said, "It's not my axe." The fairy showed him another axe made of gold and asked, "Is this the axe that you lost?" The woodcutter said, "No, it's not: My axe is made of iron. It was old." The fairy showed him the lost axe with a wooden handle. The woodcutter then said happily that it was his axe. The fairy became very pleased and gave him the gold and the silver axes too as a reward of his honesty. The wood cutter became very happy getting the axes made of gold and silver. He thanked the fairy and went home. Later, selling those two axes in the market, he made quite a good amount of money. He became solvent and started passing his days happily ever after. Thus, the honest people are rewarded everywhere.

Explanation:
Explanation: The continuation that shows the woodcutter remaining honest and being rewarded fits the opening because the story explicitly sets up his poverty and honesty, which signals a moral folktale pattern where character traits determine outcomes. Such an ending maintains narrative coherence (his honesty logically leads to a positive consequence) and reinforces the intended lesson about integrity. When completing the story, keep the tone simple, make the consequences follow naturally from his actions, and show how the choice reflects the theme.

Question #125 (ID: 209082)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Write at least teh more sentences to complete it.

Once, there was a farmer in a village. He was very idle. He had a few plots of land. But he did not plough them well. He did not sow seeds in time... ... .

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

An Idle Farmer/Consequence of Idleness

Once, there was a farmer in a village. He was very idle. He had a few plots of land. But he did not plough them well. He did not sow seeds in time. He had a kitchen garden, too. One day, he saw that the fencing round the garden was broken by a herd of goats. The farmer said, "I will repair the fence tomorrow." But the next day he would totally forget it. One day, while sitting in the yard, he noticed that some goats had entered the garden. He told his wife, who was cooking, to tend the goats. When his wife went to the garden, a dog entered the kitchen and was snatching something. She took a heavy piece of wood and threw it to the dog. The wood missed its aim and hit the little son of the farmer who was playing in the yard. The son got seriously injured. At this, the farmer understood the consequence of his idleness and promised that he would not leave today's work for tomorrow.

Explanation:
Because the opening shows the farmer’s laziness (he did not plough or sow in time), a correct continuation that describes poor harvests and the farmer’s eventual decision to work harder follows logically by cause and effect. This teaches the simple moral that effort and responsibility lead to better outcomes, so completing the story with consequences and a change in the farmer’s behavior gives a clear resolution and character development.

Question #127 (ID: 209084)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words:

Ismail Miah is an established farmer of Dhunchi, a village standing on the bank of the Padma. Though he was born in a poor family, today he is an idol to the hardworking youths of the area. One day, he told them about his success story to... ... .

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

Ismail Miah's Success

Ismail Miah is an established farmer of Dhunchi, a village standing on the bank of the Padma. Though he was born in a poor family, today he is an idol to the hardworking youths of the area. One day, he told them about his success story to illustrate how success in life only comes with hard work, perseverance and luck. He lost both his parents at a young age, so he had to take the helms of his family. He struggled to make ends meet, spending days shining shoes, and nights learning about agriculture. Then he saw an advert for a farming idea competition, where the winner would receive a grant to start his own agro venture. Fast-forward 5 years, after Ismail Miah's brilliant idea of column-based plantations won top credit, life took an uphill climb. Ismail Miah was fortunate enough to have also received training to ensure he could maximize profits while minimizing costs. Initially he had to put in 15 to 18 hours on a daily basis. However, as the days progressed, he gathered enough profits to hire help. He credited local government ventures, perseverance and hard work for his success. "But above all, I feel like you also need just a pinch of luck, and I think I had just that much!" Ismail said with a wide-toothed grin.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ইসমাইল মিয়ার কাহিনি শেষ করতে এমনভাবে লেখা উচিত যে সে তরুণদের অনুপ্রাণিত করতে, তাদের পরিশ্রম ও পরিকল্পনার গুরুত্ব বোঝাতে গল্প শেয়ার করছে; এটাই বক্তব্যের প্রাসঙ্গিকতা নিশ্চিত করে। সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে তার সংগ্রাম, সঠিক কৃষি পদ্ধতি, সঞ্চয় ও উদ্ভাবনের উদাহরণ দিলে পাঠক বুঝবে কীভাবে কঠোর পরিশ্রম ও বুদ্ধি সফলতার পথে নিয়ে যায়।

Question #128 (ID: 209085)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the following story and complete it in your own way: Give a suitable title to the story:

Fardin was an educated young man.. After completing his MA, he went to Dhaka in search of a job. He applied for various posts, but he did not get any. Being frustrated, he returned.. ... .

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans.

Fardin's Determination

Fardin was an educated young man. After completing his MA, he went to Dhaka in search of a job. He applied for various posts, but he did not get any. Being frustrated, he returned to his native village. As he was a highly qualified man he did not want to depend on others any longer. He became determined to stand on his own feet and be self-reliant. One day, one of his teachers advised him to go to an NGO and apply for micro-credit. As advised, he went to an NGO of his village and applied for micro-credit. The NGO granted him a handsome money. With the money, Fardin opened a restaurant in his village. As Fardin's mother was a great cook, she initially cooked for the restaurant. The villagers used to come to his restaurant and have food. Fardin began to earn money. Later he hired two cooks and expanded the restaurant. Soon he became solvent. Now he is one of the richest men of his village. Thus, he became an example for the young men who are qualified but jobless.

Explanation:
শিরোনাম "আশার ফেরত" — ফারদিন ঢাকায় চাকরি না পেয়ে গ্রামে ফিরে এসে নিজের শিক্ষা ও দক্ষতা কাজে লাগিয়ে টিউশন বা ছোট উদ্যোক্তা হিসেবে আত্মনির্ভর হয়ে ওঠে। এটি যুক্তিযুক্ত কারণ হতাশা থেকে পুনরুজ্জীবনের বাস্তবধর্মী পর্যায় দেখায় এবং চরিত্রের অভিজ্ঞতা ও সিদ্ধান্তের কারণ-ফল স্পষ্ট করে। গল্পের মূল ধারণা—অধ্যবসায়, বাস্তবতার সঙ্গে মানিয়ে নেওয়া এবং শিক্ষাকে ব্যবহার করে জীবন গঠন—এই সমাপ্তি ও শিরোনাম দু’টোই ভালোভাবে প্রকাশ করে।

Question #130 (ID: 209087)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The following is the beginning of a story. Complete it in your own words.

Once, there was a selfish giant who had a large and beautiful garden. The garden was full of soft green grass. Here and there all over the grass stood many colourful flowers like stars......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Selfish Giant

Once, there was a selfish giant who had a large and beautiful garden. The garden was full of soft green grass. Here and there all over the grass stood many colourful flowers like stars. The garden was a playground for the beautiful children. The children used to like the garden very much. So, they came to the garden every day to play different kinds of games. But they did not know that the selfish giant was the owner of the garden. They came and played as usual. Suddenly the giant noticed the children playing in his garden. Then he planned to make a big wall so that they could not enter the garden. Ultimately he made a big wall. As a result, the children coming near the garden could not enter into it. In the meantime, the garden had been flowerless and grass less. It was losing its beauty gradually. The selfish giant thought himself of the matter. At this he got into a great tension and tried to find out the real cause behind it. At last, he realized his mistakes and said to himself, "Children are the great blessings of the garden". He called the children, made a good relationship with them andloved them from his core of heart. He allowed them to enter the garden and play again. Then the garden started to get back its beauty slowly. And eventually, it became the same as like as it was before. Thus, the selfish giant gained self-knowledge and self-realization through his mistakes.

Explanation:
The correct ending shows the giant’s change from selfishness to kindness because the opening—his beautiful garden and his exclusion of children—sets up a moral lesson about sharing and compassion. Bringing children back and letting the garden bloom again demonstrates cause and effect (loneliness from selfishness versus joy from kindness) and gives the giant clear character growth. This resolution matches the story’s imagery and teaches that love and generosity restore life and happiness.

Ismail Miah's Success

Ismail Miah is an established farmer of Dhunchi, a village standing on the bank of the Padma. Though he was born in a poor family, today he is an idol to the hardworking youths of the area. One day, he told them about his success story to illustrate how success in life only comes with hard work, perseverance and luck. He lost both his parents at a young age, so he had to take the helms of his family. He struggled to make ends meet, spending days shining shoes, and nights learning about agriculture. Then he saw an advert for a farming idea competition, where the winner would receive a grant to start his own agro venture. Fast-forward 5 years, after Ismail Miah's brilliant idea of column-based plantations won top credit, life took an uphill climb. Ismail Miah was fortunate enough to have also received training to ensure he could maximize profits while minimizing costs. Initially he had to put in 15 to 18 hours on a daily basis. However, as the days progressed, he gathered enough profits to hire help. He credited local government ventures, perseverance and hard work for his success. "But above all, I feel like you also need just a pinch of luck, and I think I had just that much!" Ismail said with a wide-toothed grin.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক উত্তরটি বলে যে ইসমাইল মিয়া যুবকদের উৎসাহ দিতে ও তাদের কাজ ও উপায়-কৌশল শিখাতে নিজের সফলতার গল্প বললেন, কারণ তার দরিদ্র থেকে সফল হওয়ার বাস্তব অভিজ্ঞতা তাদের জন্য অনুপ্রেরণা ও ব্যবহারযোগ্য শিক্ষা দেয়। গল্পের মূল ধারণা হল চরিত্রের গতিবিধি ও নৈতিক শিক্ষা দেখানো—এমন শেষ অংশ বেছে নিতে হবে যেটা তাঁর পরিশ্রম, সঠিক পরিকল্পনা ও আধুনিক কৃষি অনুশীলনের গুরুত্ব বোঝায় এবং পাঠকদের প্রেরণা দেয়।

Question #132 (ID: 209089)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Write at least teh more sentences to complete it.

Once, there was a farmer in a village. He was very idle. He had a few plots of land. But he did not plough them well. He did not sow seeds in time.......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
An Idle Farmer/Consequence of Idleness

Once, there was a farmer in a village. He was very idle. He had a few plots of land. But he did not plough them well. He did not sow seeds in time. He had a kitchen garden, too. One day, he saw that the fencing round the garden was broken by a herd of goats. The farmer said, "I will repair the fence tomorrow." But the next day he would totally forget it. One day, while sitting in the yard, he noticed that some goats had entered the garden. He told his wife, who was cooking, to tend the goats. When his wife went to the garden, a dog entered the kitchen and was snatching something. She took a heavy piece of wood and threw it to the dog. The wood missed its aim and hit the little son of the farmer who was playing in the yard. The son got seriously injured. At this, the farmer understood the consequence of his idleness and promised that he would not leave today's work for tomorrow.

Explanation:
The correct continuation should show the consequences of the farmer’s idleness (poor or no harvest) and then either his suffering or a lesson learned. This is right because the opening sets up a clear cause (neglecting the land), so a natural effect and a moral resolution follow, which makes the story coherent. That structure helps students see cause-and-effect and understand the theme of responsibility.

Question #133 (ID: 209090)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story.

There was a pond full of frogs. Some of them often put their heads out of the water and croaked loudly. One day, some boys were playing by the side of the pond. When they heard the frogs croaking......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ans to the Q. no. 8

The Naughty Boys and the Frogs

There was an old pond in a village. It was full of frogs. The frogs were living happily there. Some of them often put their heads out of the water and croaked loudly. One day, some boys were playing by the side of the pond. When they heard the frogs croaking, they started throwing stones at the frogs and made fun. The stone hit the frogs. As a result, some frogs were killed and many were wounded. The frogs were very much puzzled and did not know what to do. At last, an old frog raised its head and said, "Dear little boys, why are you killing us?" The boys said, "We are not killing you. We are just playing." Then the frog said, "What is play to you is death to us." The boys became very sorry and ashamed. So, they stopped their game and left the place.

Explanation:
উত্তরটি ঠিক কারণ এটি গল্পের শুরু থেকে ধারাবাহিকভাবে ঘটনাপ্রবাহ বজায় রেখেছে—ছেলেদের আগমন, ব্যস্ততা এবং সেটার ফলে ব্যাঙদের প্রতিক্রিয়া দেখায়—এবং আঁচড়ে শেষ পর্যন্ত একটি পরিষ্কার ফলাফল বা ন্যায়নীতি দিয়েছে। এছাড়া নির্দেশমতো কমপক্ষে দশটি নতুন বাক্য যোগ করা হয়েছে, তাই প্রশ্নের শর্ত পূরণ করে। মূল ধারণা হলো একটি সংহত কাহিনি গঠনের জন্য শুরু, সংঘাত এবং সমাধান থাকা দরকার যাতে পাঠক সহজে কারণ-ফল ও নৈতিক শিক্ষা বুঝতে পারে।

Question #134 (ID: 506793)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Leaves tumble in late October: they glitter in a brief sun, are lauded by children and passed along the lane, then rot unseen beneath the frost. The passerby praises their color, then slips onward when the chill bites. A small rhyme repeats: "Applaud the gold, then forget the hold."

Options:
ক. এই প্রস্তুতিটির মূল ভাব বা থিম কী?
খ. প্যারাগ্রাফে ব্যবহৃত দুইটি সাহিত্যিক অলঙ্কার চিহ্নিত করো ও সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করো।
গ. "Applaud the gold, then forget the hold" এই লাইনটির অর্থ কী?
ঘ. প্যাসেজের টোন কিরূপ এবং কীভাবে সেটি গঠিত হয়েছে?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: প্রধান ভাব হলো প্রকৃতির অল্পস্থায়ী সৌন্দর্যকে মানুষের অস্থায়ী প্রশংসা ও অনুগামীতায় তুলনা করে মানুষের অনুগৃহীততা ও ভ্রান্ত পরিচর্যার প্রতি সমালোচনা। এখানে শীত আগােভাবেই মানুষের প্রত্যাহার ও উপেক্ষাকে প্রকৃতির ক্ষয়ক্ষতির সঙ্গে মিলিয়ে দেখানো হয়েছে।

খ উত্তর: 1) ব্যক্তিত্বদান (Personification): পাতা যেন মানুষ দ্বারা প্রশংসা পাওয়া ও ভুলে যাওয়ার মতো আচরণ করে — প্রকৃতি বা অজীব বস্তুকে মানবীয় গুণ দেওয়া হয়েছে। 2) বিপর্যয়বচকতা/ইরনি (Irony): পাতা তার চূড়ান্ত সৌন্দর্যে প্রশংসিত হয়, অথচ সেই প্রশংসা দীর্ঘস্থায়ী নয়; প্রশংসিত হওয়া সত্ত্বেও অবহেলায় পড়ে।

গ উত্তর: লাইনটির সাংগঠনিক অর্থ হলো: লোকেরা যখন কোনো জিনিস বা ব্যক্তির ঝলমলে দিক দেখে তখন তাতেই প্রশংসা করে, কিন্তু সত্যিকারের সংযোগ বা সহায়তা (the "hold") দেয় না; তারা ফুসফুসণভাবে বা অস্থায়ীভাবে সাদরে নেয় কিন্তু পরে তা ভুলে যায় বা ত্যাগ করে। এখানে "gold" সৌন্দর্য/সম্মান বোঝায় এবং "hold" স্থায়ী সমর্থন বা কৃতজ্ঞতা বোঝায়।

ঘ উত্তর: টোনটি ভাবগাম্ভীর্যপূর্ণ ও সামান্য নীরস; এতে হতাশা ও তীব্র সচেতনতার ছোঁয়া আছে। এটি গঠিত হয়েছে সংক্ষিপ্ত, চিত্রপূর্ণ বর্ণনা, পুনরাবৃত্ত রাইশ (refrain) এবং প্রকৃতির অস্থায়ীত্বকে মানুষের অনিন্দ্য আচরণের সঙ্গে মিলিয়ে ব্যাখ্যার মাধ্যমে।

Explanation:
বহুবিধ উপাদান—প্রকৃতির চিত্রায়ন, সংক্ষিপ্ত রৈখিক বিবরণ ও পুনরাবৃত্ত শ্লোক—মিলিয়ে প্যাসেজটি মানুষের অস্থায়ী প্রশংসা ও অনুগৃহীততার রাজনৈতিক ও নৈতিক দিক তুলে ধরে। ব্যক্তিত্বদান ও ইরনি ব্যবহার করে লেখক পাঠককে অনুভব করাতে চান যে যে যা দীপ্ত সেখানে স্থায়িত্ব নেই, বরং মানবিক সম্পর্কের অবনতি প্রকৃতির পতনের মতোই তীব্র।
